▲ Tokyo, October 19 (Dentsu) The Kokumin Domei (National League) studied its attitude toward next year's budget, with Chairman Adachi at the center. Yesterday's standing committee reached a general conclusion. Adachi issued a statement in the form of a talk, as follows: "The government's budget compilation policy does not seek any new solutions to the root causes of today's stalemate, but only leaves behind doubled harm for the future. According to the government's budget, it will issue 1 billion yen in deficit bonds. If this continues, the total amount of public debt will reach 10 billion yen, and all tax revenue will be taken up by public debt interest and pensions. The future of public finance is extremely worrying. It is heard that the government also fears criticism from the world and has a plan to establish a financial advisory body. However, starting the investigation at this point will only waste time and will not be enough to address the current extraordinary financial situation. It is necessary to compile an extraordinary budget that saves both the internal and external situation, and at the same time, to carry out fundamental political and economic reforms. However, given the weakness of the current cabinet, how can we expect such a major reform? We believe that the most urgent task at hand is the emergence of a truly powerful emergency cabinet with the mission of saving the situation."

▲ Tokyo, October 19 (Dentsu) Minister of Education Hatoyama visited Minister of Finance Takahashi yesterday afternoon at the behest of President Suzuki of the Seiyūkai (Friends of Constitutional Government Party) to ask for his views on next year's budget and his confidence in the Diet. The Minister of Finance replied that looking at the situation in other countries, there is no need to be so pessimistic about issuing deficit bonds. I have resolved to sacrifice myself in this difficult situation and will face the regular Diet session with this determination. After exchanging opinions, Minister of Education Hatoyama left at 3:00 PM. At 5:00 PM, Secretary-General Matsuno and Chief Secretary Yamaguchi of the Seiyūkai visited Minister of Education Hatoyama to hear the details of the meeting with Finance Minister Takahashi. They then held important discussions on their attitude towards the government. However, because there is various criticism of the budget in the world, and the Seiyūkai's position cannot be to attack the government head-on, the relationship between the Seiyūkai and the government is very delicate. The Seiyūkai attaches great importance to Premier Saitō's visit to Prince Saionji and expects a great deal from his subsequent meeting with President Suzuki. Therefore, they plan to observe the situation before deciding on their attitude towards the budget.

▲ Tokyo, October 19 (Dentsu) The second naval replenishment plan for the 1933 fiscal year is 43.85 million yen. However, the total naval budget reaches 460 million yen, so the financial burden for the next year is very large. As a result of consultations between Premier Saitō, Navy Minister Okada, and Finance Minister Takahashi, the original plan was withdrawn and replaced with the following plan: three special-purpose ships, construction costs of 15 million yen, and ship modification costs of 26.0688 million yen, which will be compensated by the revival of approved funds. The distribution of the revived approved funds of 45 million yen is roughly as follows: 35.0688 million yen for the above two planned expenses, 6.563 million yen for exchange rate losses, and 2.649 million yen for other expenses. Furthermore, the Navy insists that a portion of the second replenishment plan be included in the 1934 budget, but the Ministry of Finance is reluctant due to financial constraints, so it is feared that it will be difficult to realize.

▲ Tokyo, October 19 (Hua Lian News Agency) Since the Japanese exchange rate against the US dollar fell again yesterday, the market remains sluggish. The afternoon closing fell to a recent selling price of 19 and 3/4 US cents, breaking the 20 US cent barrier. According to observations by Japanese financial circles, there are four reasons for the fall in the exchange rate: 1. Due to the fall in the US stock market; 2. The League of Nations' sentiment towards Japan has deteriorated, and Japan is becoming increasingly isolated internationally; 3. Implementing the troop increase in northern Manchuria has become an unavoidable situation, and there is still pessimism about the future of the troop increase;

4. Japan's foreign trade surplus has decreased significantly, etc.

▲ Tokyo, October 19 (Hua Lian News Agency) The Japanese political situation is very stable on the surface, but there are deep undercurrents. The League of Nations situation is also not optimistic. The military and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are gradually becoming antagonistic. The zaibatsu (financial cliques) are very concerned about the future of public finances, and their attitude is increasingly different from that of the military. The brewing of the confrontation between the military and the financial cliques is becoming more and more serious.

Important Telegrams

Soviet Russian Correspondence (Sent from Vladivostok, October 28) 63

▲ The World's Largest Hydroelectric Power Plant, the Dnieper Hydroelectric Station, Opens

▲ Moscow's Views and Inspections of the Lytton Report

▲ The Question of the Soviet Russian and Romanian Signing of a Non-Aggression Treaty

The Dnieper Hydroelectric Station, a central project in the Soviet Russian Five-Year Plan and watched by the whole world, officially opened on the 10th of this month. The Dnieper Dam and all its affiliated projects began in November 1927 and have taken exactly five years to complete. It used more than 15,000 workers and cost 800 million rubles. The power plant can supply 810,000 horsepower and 3 billion kilowatt-hours of electricity per year. All industries and transportation in the new industrial area, as well as the metallurgical industry in southern Ukraine, rely on it for electricity. It is truly one of the world's largest hydroelectric projects. A grand opening ceremony was held on the 10th of this month. The chairman of the Soviet Russian Workers' and Peasants' Government, Mr. Kalinin, together with the chairman of the Industrial Committee, Mr. Osokini, were guided by the chief engineer, Mr. Ventzel, and Mr. Michelson to inspect the dam on the evening of the 9th. At a height of 60 meters above the Dnieper River, Lenin's last words were projected: "Soviet power plus electrification is socialism." On the right bank of the river, Stalin's words, "The Bolsheviks are invincible," were also projected. Tens of thousands of people, guests, government representatives, diplomatic representatives, and journalists from Moscow, Charkov, and other places attended the grand event. Special trains were opened to travel to the opening ceremony. At the opening ceremony, Chief Engineer Ventzel gave a speech reporting on the progress of the project. Then, Mr. Kalinin, chairman of the Workers' and Peasants' Government, gave a speech on behalf of the government, thanking the construction workers, engineers, and foreign experts for their cooperation in enabling the Soviet Russian construction plan to be completed on schedule. Mr. Kalinin immediately announced the resolution of the Workers' and Peasants' Government to name the power plant "Lenin Hydroelectric Power Plant." The crowd cheered and accepted. After Mr. Kalinin's speech, Mr. Chubar gave a speech on behalf of the Federal and Ukrainian governments on the relationship between the power plant and the development of new industries and the consolidation of the new regime. Then, Colonel Cooper, the chief consulting engineer from the United States, gave a speech praising the Russian government's perseverance and the boundless future of New Russia. Mr. Cooper also said that this construction was tantamount to training tens of thousands of engineers for New Russia, and its significance for the future was not limited to the completion of a large power plant. Among the guests who spoke was the world-renowned literary figure Henri Barbusse. Finally, Mr. Kalinin, on behalf of the government, awarded medals to a total of 67 people who had made special contributions to this project, including six foreign experts (namely, Chief Consultant Cooper, Engineer Faber, Engineer McFee, Chief Engineer Ventzel, Engineer Thompson, and Engineer Pindell), all of whom received the Order of the Red Banner. Colonel Cooper was given a certificate of merit by the Workers' and Peasants' Government for his special contributions. Among these 67 people, there were also two women. A monument to their merits was erected inside the plant, with the names of 16 people engraved on it, with Cooper at the head, and Ventzel and others included. On that day, the plant received thousands of congratulatory telegrams from home and abroad, including a telegram from the American Institute of Engineers in Newburgh. The joy of those involved in the project, the enthusiasm of the crowd, and the praise of the diplomatic representatives and journalists made the event a memorable one in history. In 1920, the famous British writer H.G. Wells visited Lenin in the Kremlin and published his impression that the new Russian leaders had many fantasies and that success was difficult. He was particularly critical of the electrification plan, saying that it would be difficult to succeed. Unexpectedly, it was completed on schedule. It is said that the Niagara Falls power plant in the United States can only supply 430,000 horsepower, and the largest Tennessee River hydroelectric plant in North America can only supply 620,000 horsepower, while the Dnieper plant can supply 810,000 horsepower, making it the world's largest hydroelectric power plant.

××××××

After the publication of the Lytton Report, the Moscow Weekly published a lengthy editorial attacking it as a "wonderful article of anti-China, anti-Russian, and anti-Japanese," combining the conflicts between imperialist countries and the hostility between imperialism and Soviet Russia. The editorial stated that the role of this document was not to solve world disputes or ensure peace, but to plunge the disputes into deeper waters, making the prospects for peace even more embarrassing. The editorial pointed out that this report had set a precedent in international disputes, allowing countries with aggressive intentions to act boldly in the future, while small and weak nations would be placed in an even more precarious position. This was tantamount to the League of Nations openly recognizing the legitimacy of aggression, and the League's facade of guaranteeing peace and sanctioning aggression had been completely exposed. The Lytton Report's attitude towards Manchuria as Chinese territory seemed to be one of recognition, but it was hesitant and full of reservations. The editorial did not spare any ridicule. The anti-Russian parts of the report were very obvious, but the author believed that this report was not only anti-China and anti-Russian, but also fully anti-Japanese. The League of Nations did not need to care about the interests of the Chinese, and it was bound to be hostile to Soviet Russia, but it also did not want the Japanese to swallow this piece of fat alone. Therefore, the international committee it proposed was intended to prevent Japan from swallowing it alone and to allow the imperialist powers to share the benefits. Therefore, the author believes that this document is consistent with the original nature of the League of Nations, and its significance is nothing more than expressing the conflicts between the imperialist countries themselves, the hostility towards Russia, and the oppression of small and weak nations. Its role is to add fuel to the fire, and the prospect of peace will soon be in crisis. On October 13, the newspaper Izvestia published an article by Radek, an expert on Eastern issues, commenting on the Lytton Report, saying that Japan's forceful occupation of Manchuria also had its "difficulties." It knew that it would be difficult to compete with the European and American imperialist powers by peacefully invading China, so it had to resort to rapid means. The Lytton Commission was not satisfied with this, so the report acknowledged that the establishment of Manchuria was purely the work of the Japanese, which clearly criticized their actions. Radek said that after the Manchurian Incident, the conflict between the United States and Japan had reached a point of intense excitement. Britain and France were trying their best to deal with Japan, wanting to use it as a vanguard to confront the United States. Since the United States wanted to achieve its goals, it could not but be on good terms with Britain and France. Therefore, the recent negotiations between Britain and France on the war debt issue have resumed, and this will be used as a condition for wooing and supporting Germany. However, according to Radek's observation, it is still uncertain whether the coordination between Britain and France and the United States can ultimately be realized, as there are many hidden reefs between them. Although Davis's recent trip to London and British Admiral Chatfield's trip to the United States can prove that they are continuing to work tirelessly, it is difficult to say that there have been significant results.

Among the countries neighboring Soviet Russia, Poland and Romania have been the most hostile to Soviet Russia and have been used by other countries to be eager to move against Russia. Poland has recently concluded a non-aggression treaty with Soviet Russia, but negotiations between Soviet Russia and Romania have been going on for ten months, but have been interrupted repeatedly and have not yet produced any results. In July, Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov planned to continue negotiations with Romanian representatives in Switzerland, but was unsuccessful. Afterwards, the mediation of Poland was resumed, but the points of disagreement between the two sides could not be coordinated. Soviet Russia wanted to retain its original attitude towards the unresolved issues between the two countries, while Romania firmly opposed this and was unwilling to include it in the treaty. Therefore, from Soviet Russia's perspective, Romania's attitude was tantamount to wanting Soviet Russia to recognize its occupation of Bessarabia under the guise of a non-aggression treaty. When Russia and Romania negotiated in Riga, they broke down because of this issue. Recently, when Litvinov went to Geneva in September, he said that Poland, through the mediation of the Polish ambassador to Romania, Katai, had gradually approached each other on the points of disagreement. After repeated negotiations in Switzerland, their views had become extremely close and were about to be signed. The next day, the Romanian representative suddenly claimed that the Romanian government could not agree and revoked all the agreed opinions, and then it was interrupted again. At present, the Romanian government has not made any other statement on this, so it seems that their views are still difficult to approach, and the issue of signing a treaty with Russia is feared that it will be difficult to realize for a while.

The Public in Geneva is Waiting Silently for Rain to Come 64

▲ The Subtleties of the Lytton Report

Geneva Correspondence The 13th General Assembly of the League of Nations closed on October 17 in a spiritless mood. The Manchurian problem, which was watched by all eyes, was postponed for four weeks at the request of Japan. Alas, the League is nearing its end.

In the West, thirteen is considered unlucky. This session happened to coincide with the increasingly acute Sino-Japanese dispute, which almost shook the very foundation of the League. It seems that there is a destiny in the dark. In fact, the League has long become a League of Europe. It does not want to hear about this kind of East Asian problem from the bottom of its heart. However, China has already raised the issue and relies on it with all its might, so in order to maintain its appearance, it has no words to refuse. Moreover, many small and weak countries that are neighbors with strong countries are shuddering at Japan's undeclared war, which set a bad precedent after the European War. Therefore, representatives from countries such as Czechoslovakia and Spain shouted loudly in the Administrative Council, directly scolding Japan as a leader of rebels and urging the Chinese representative to propose Article 16 of the League Covenant to punish it. And it is said to people that we are not helping China but helping ourselves. If there is no league, we will not be able to sleep peacefully. The League's benefit is to turn big things into small things and small things into nothing, but they insist on expanding the scope and increasing the intensity. This makes the paper tiger that maintains world peace headache and helpless.

Since the publication of the Lytton Report, the world has welcomed it with great interest. Different countries have different positions, so the criticisms are extremely inconsistent. Britain and Germany have an ambiguous attitude and are neither here nor there. The United States sees Britain as a shift and hopes for joint action. Italy says that it is a huge work of perfunctory for both sides, and the result is still equal to zero. France says that the current situation is caused by internal chaos in China, which is unavoidable. Russia says that placing Manchuria under international co-management is tantamount to provoking it. From our perspective, the investigation by a third party proves that Japan's violation of all treaties is superficially not unfavorable to China, such as saying that (1) the pending cases that Japan has used as an excuse are not true; (2) the September 18th Incident was not Japan's self-defense; (3) all of Japan's actions were premeditated; (4) "Manchukuo" was forged by Japan and was not the intention of the Chinese people. The recommendations not only advocate that Japan withdraw its troops, but also withdraw all its troops along the South Manchurian Railway. Seeking the opposite of the wording has already clearly declared Japan's guilt, that is, it is aggression rather than self-defense, and it destroys China's territorial integrity rather than the intention of the people of Northeast China. What is regrettable is that after finding out that the responsibility for the September 18th Incident lies entirely with Japan, it is again induced by practical interests, hoping that it will compromise with China. The League of Nations had already ordered Japan to withdraw its troops long ago.

Page 10

There are brilliant proposals to be examined, but it is again advocated that neither China nor Japan should station troops in Northeast China, and that the international cooperation should be included in the transformation of China. All of this is self-contradictory and cannot be self-justified. The greatest key to thinking of this compromise solution in the situation where the force of aggression has become a matter of the moment is to center on the interests of the great powers themselves. Therefore, after careful deliberation of the report, it is found that it is concerned about the details. At present, it is using China's generosity to give Japan small favors, making the Northeast portal wide open, and not allowing one person to monopolize it. As a result, Japan will inevitably be trapped in a poor and isolated island, and it will be difficult to realize its dream of a continental policy. Therefore, if the suggestions are implemented one by one, it will be a lose-lose situation for China and Japan. Japan is determined to dominate East Asia and control the universe, and this kind of ambition will never be easily expressed in the future. Even the small favors obtained from China will be divided by the great powers. China will be at the mercy of others and lose its freedom, and there is no escape from the immediate loss. Alas, it is to be feared.

It is necessary to mention the recent situation in Europe. Germany's demand for military equality is tantamount to confronting France with an arrow, so the whereabouts of Davis and Herriot are the most noticeable. Is it a four-power meeting, a three-power meeting, Lausanne or The Hague? When I was writing this article, negotiations were still continuing. France wants to maintain its vested interests, so it is beneficial to maintain the covenant. Germany is the opposite. Although Britain is a mediator on the surface, the actual influence can be left to the United States. Japan's occupation of Manchuria clearly violates the open door policy. The United States wants to maintain the dignity of its Pacific policy, so it is happy to have the same guarantee as France. Therefore, if a turnaround can be obtained in the disarmament issue, Europe can temporarily get a small well-being and can divide its attention to East Asia. Japan may be able to restrain itself slightly under international supervision.

"All trees are silent, waiting for the rain to come." This is the recent situation in Geneva. The Japanese delegation has been led by Yosuke Matsuoka, who advocates the internationalization of Shanghai, and Isamu Yoshida, who accompanied the investigation team to Northeast China. Therefore, the saying that Japan will withdraw from the League is enough to prove that it is just empty talk and intimidation. At the same time, he hired an American, Bruwnson Rea, the chief writer of the Shanghai Far Eastern Times, to come here to promote it. One night, he entertained reporters from various countries and stated that he was a representative of "Manchukuo." The Americans scoffed at him, and a Chinese reporter directly rebuked him, saying, I know that what I represent is not "Manchukuo" but money. Rea was embarrassed and angry, so he turned off the lights and left. The Japanese have been using heavy money to win over reporters from various countries to help them spread rumors, and they have also published two books in English and French to slander China, one named "The Present Condition of China" and the other named "Relations of Japan with Manchuria and Mongolia," and distributed them to bookstores and newsstands for sale without taking any value. Other similar methods are too numerous to mention. The Chinese delegation, fearing that the world would be deceived by one-sided words, had no choice but to prepare several publications describing the Japanese national conditions and the truth of the military's arrogance, proving that it was not necessarily an organized country, and waited for the conference to distribute them. According to those who are familiar with the Japanese situation, the Japanese will definitely not accept the Lytton Report and will take delaying tactics and shirk their responsibility to China, saying, "Even if I accept the report, there is no one on the other side who can contact me. Does the government have this power?"

The Chinese delegation rented No. 18 Rue Charles Gallond as an office. Representative Yan Huiqing also lives in it. Other representatives and staff either live in hotels or apartments. The daily expenses are only enough to match the Japanese delegation's car expenses. In addition to Yan Huiqing as the chief representative at next month's conference, Gu Weijun and Guo Taiqi will also be added as representatives. Gu, who accompanied the investigation team to Northeast China, has been internally scheduled to attend the Executive Council first and explain the Northeast problem at any time. In addition, there are also Deputy Representative Luo Zongyi, Minister to Denmark, Jin Wensi, Minister to the Netherlands, Hu Shize, Representative to Switzerland, and Liang Long, Counselor of the Embassy in Germany. Special Committee Members Xu Shuxi, Professor of Yenching University, Wang Dazhen, Chief Writer of Diplomacy Monthly, Yan Deqing, Technical Supervisor of the Ministry of Railways, Qian Tai, Director of the International Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Shen Jinding, Director of the Asian Department, and Xia Jinlin, First Secretary of the Embassy in England, are assisting from the side.

Combining the opinions of most Chinese and foreign people, it is said that the Northeast problem was not caused in a short period of time, so it cannot be solved in one day. Hoping that the League will recover the lost land for China is nothing but idle talk on paper. Today, the only way out for China is to summon talented people to the capital to strengthen the government and take responsibility, and at the same time, to fully support the volunteer army and resist Japanese goods. There is no other good strategy than this. As the saying goes, heaven helps those who help themselves. Even if Japan is unrepentant or the League is willing to sacrifice to help, China must at least show that it has the ability to manipulate everything in the future. Therefore, we look forward to it not for diplomatic victory but for internal unity, and instead of hating foreigners for being unfair, we should cheer up and do some construction work to stop the mouths of those who curse. We should know that if there is no way to deal with internal affairs, there will be no way to deal with external affairs. (Geneva, October 15)

A Certain Friendly Nation Diplomat's Commentary on the Japanese Memorandum 65

▲ Foreign Minister Luo Will Also Draft a Refutation of the Declaration

The League of Nations Investigation Commission's report on the September 18th Incident clarified that Japan's military actions were not in self-defense. The establishment of the puppet organization was also proven to be the result of Japanese military force and not the will of the people of the Northeast Three Provinces. Japan's violation of the League of Nations Covenant and all other conventions has been revealed to the world. Therefore, the Japanese side has vehemently opposed the report and produced a memorandum openly insulting our country, even claiming that our country has no unified government. This absurd and outrageous memorandum was submitted to the League of Nations on the 18th and its summary was released by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited a diplomat from a certain friendly nation who has resided in China for many years to inquire about his opinion on the Japanese memorandum. He provided a detailed response, which is recorded as follows:

▲ Japan's Forceful Arguments Seek to Conceal the Truth: The diplomat began by saying to the reporter that he had seen the summary of the memorandum released by Tokyo on the 18th regarding the Investigation Commission's report. He stated that its wording and intentions were extremely absurd. The purpose of the Japanese memorandum was to evade responsibility for the September 18th Incident, hoping to overturn the truthful and impartial record of the Manchurian Incident in the report. Furthermore, it attempted to insult China as a country without a unified government, even claiming that China is not a country but merely a geographical term. It sought to evade responsibility for violating international conventions and shift international opinion. However, the League of Nations has long been aware of this situation and has decided to deny the so-called "Manchukuo" based on the Lytton Report. Currently, Japan feels isolated in the international environment, and representatives of various countries in Geneva oppose the "Manchukuo" created single-handedly by Japan, as it hinders peace in the Far East. The Japanese memorandum only reveals its attempt to conceal the truth.

▲ Japan Insults the Entire Chinese Nation: The diplomat continued by saying that he has resided in China for a long time and is deeply aware that China's current situation is a phase in the process of construction. There is absolutely no country that can be denied its status as a country simply because it has some internal strife. The establishment of the National Government in Nanjing is a fact recognized by all nations of the world. The Japanese memorandum's claim that China has no unified government is a great insult to the entire Chinese nation. The reporter further inquired whether the Japanese memorandum's claim that Japan's bombing of Jinzhou was a legitimate action recognized by the Hague Convention was true, and whether the Hague Convention indeed permits military aggression as a legitimate action. The diplomat replied that any international convention is based on universal principles, in other words, international conventions are international justice. The reporter asked what the Japanese referred to as a legitimate action recognized by the Hague Convention. The diplomat laughed and replied that he did not know.

▲ Foreign Minister Luo Will Draft a Declaration to Refute It: The reporter also learned that Foreign Minister Luo Wengan has decided to draft a declaration to refute the absurdity of the Japanese memorandum, which is currently being drafted and will be officially released soon. (Central News Agency)

Two Lius Accuse Each Other of Victory 66

▲ Liu Xiang Cables Claiming Occupation of Fushun and Neijiang

▲ Liu Wenhui Cables Claiming Victory Over Enemy in Luzhou

Hankou Correspondence: Liu Xiang, Commander of the 21st Army, launched a large-scale offensive with land, sea, and air forces against Luzhou. The 24th Army under Liu Wenhui, stationed in Luzhou, made every effort to resist, engaging in intense combat. In the past ten days, dozens of battles, large and small, have resulted in heavy losses on both sides. Liu Xiang's army suffered particularly heavy casualties during numerous attempts to cross the river, all of which were repelled. Liu Wenhui urgently ordered Yang Shangzhou and Tian Zhongyi's brigades to defend their positions and also dispatched Gao Ruming's brigade to reinforce them. Liu Xiang, realizing that Luzhou would not be easily captured, turned to attack Longtouguan, five miles from Luzhou. Meanwhile, he launched simultaneous offensives with heavy forces directly towards Neijiang and Fushun, with fierce fighting reported on all fronts. According to a cable from Chengdu on the 17th, the front lines remained unchanged, and the two sides were still in a stalemate. However, on the 18th, Liu Xiang cabled, claiming that both Neijiang and Fushun had been captured. The original telegram stated: 1) My Wang Zhiyi's troops occupied Neijiang at noon today. 2) Tang Shizun and Pan Wenhua's two divisions occupied Fushun today, and Xu Yaoqing's brigade occupied Ziliujing. 3) In the Luzhou area, Longtouguan has been occupied, and Liu Wenhui's retreat route has been cut off. Luzhou City can be expected to be captured within days. 4) Fierce fighting between Tian and Liu's armies is taking place near the Thatched Cottage and the Wuhou Temple near Chengdu. 5) Liu Wenhui's troops, disregarding their flanks, have been largely disarmed. The Sichuan war is expected to be resolved in the shortest possible time. According to those familiar with the Sichuan situation, Liu Wenhui's troops are very determined. Whether victory or defeat can be decided in a single day remains to be seen. We dare not lightly believe it without factual proof. However, while confronting Liu Xiang's army, Liu Wenhui still expressed his desire for peace. On the 9th, he telegraphed the central government and Chairman Chiang, requesting that they stop the arrogance and end the war. On the 15th, he telegraphed the National Government, the various ministries, and Chairman Chiang, reporting on the situation of the Chongqing army's advance, stating, "According to reports from Yang Shangzhou and Tian Zhongyi, brigade commanders in Luzhou, on the [date], the enemy army has been bombarding Luzhou City for days, using sulfur bombs to burn down civilian houses. Today, from midnight to noon, the infantry, in addition to the original six brigades, added two special forces regiments and five airplanes, along with one warship and five merchant ships, covered about sixty or seventy wooden boats to launch fierce attacks on three fronts, land, sea, and air, divided into dozens of teams to force a crossing, advancing one after another. Our army, with one against ten, fought bravely, resisting fiercely, making it the first fierce battle since the start of the war in Luzhou. When the enemy forced a crossing, our army calmly responded, waiting for half of them to land before concentrating a large force to sweep the landing enemy. Except for those killed, all were captured without exception. Two enemy ships and ten wooden boats were sunk, and three regimental commanders, Wu Shoushan, and three battalion commanders, Xu Shaoyan, etc., were killed. More than ten regimental, battalion, and company commanders were captured, and thousands of enemy officers and soldiers were drowned. More than 500 enemy rifles and more than ten machine guns were seized. As for the losses of our army, they will be reported separately after investigation. The most tragic thing is that when the airplane bombs fall, flesh and blood fly everywhere, and houses are reduced to ashes. The wounded and dead are innocent civilians, and the devastated are the essence of the land. Looking up to the south, our hearts are cut. According to a report from brigade commander Zhang Zhifang on the [date], the enemy in front of our brigade used machine guns and mortars last night to continuously fire on our river crossing points, but failed. Today, they continued to exchange fire. At 9:00 PM, airplanes dropped nine bombs, causing great damage to people and houses. It is said that the enemy who fought fiercely with our Huang regiment at Gaoshikan had nine regiments, and more than 700 have been killed or wounded. According to a telegram from the brigade commander on the [date], the enemy launched a fierce attack on our guard points at the river crossing points at 1:00 AM today, especially at the east, south, and north gates of Fucheng. Our officers and soldiers bravely resisted and the enemy made no progress. However, more than 40 enemy bombs fell in the city, killing and injuring more than 80 people, and destroying many civilian houses. Many enemies were killed or fell into the water. At 9:00 AM, the enemy again tried to force a crossing at Pipa Field and two fishing boats were sunk by our forces. The two sides are still fighting along the river. At 2:00 PM, enemy planes came to drop three bombs, causing fires in several places, and the people cried out in shock. The situation is extremely tragic, etc. After several fierce battles, the enemy has suffered heavy losses and has not succeeded. Luzhou and Fushun are still safe. Since noon yesterday, the situation on the front line has become calm. It is expected that the enemy's intention will not be easily abandoned. When reinforcements arrive, the battle will be even more fierce. It is unexpected that Liu Xiang would act so perversely. His brutality is no different from that of foreign invaders in our country. Your Excellency is concerned about the legacy of your children and must also feel deeply grieved and unwilling to sit idly by and let the land be devastated. You must take action as soon as possible. Furthermore, there is no change in the Qiongzhou area. Neijiang is still in Peimu Town, 30 miles from the city, and the two sides are firing across the river. Sincerely telegraphed, respectfully awaiting instructions. Liu Wenhui respectfully bowed and deleted the seals." (November 18th)

Han Sends Zhang Yue to Wuhan to See Chiang 67

▲ Liu's Troops to be Downsized in Jiaodong and Then Sent to Zhejiang

Jinan Correspondence: The Jiaodong incident has been resolved, and the provincial troops have completed their withdrawal. Liu Zhennian's troops will also leave Shandong Province soon. Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, had previously indicated that he would go to Nanjing and Wuhan to report to the Central Government and Chairman Chiang on the beginning and end of the Jiaodong incident and the difficulties of using troops. Now, due to being busy with affairs, he cannot spare the time, so he first sent Provincial Commissioner Zhang Yue. Zhang, carrying a personal letter from Han, left Jinan for Beijing this morning (17th) and will transfer to Wuhan. According to Han's remarks, Zhang Yue's mission to the south is roughly as follows: I originally intended to personally go to Wuhan to meet Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and report on the Jiaodong incident. However, according to recent reports from various counties in Jiaodong, there are often remnants of Liu's troops forming gangs and becoming bandits. Moreover, after Liu's troops are transferred, a large-scale clearing of the countryside and post-war reconstruction must be carried out. I cannot leave for the time being, so I first sent Commissioner Zhang. As for the transfer of Liu Zhennian's troops, it is heard that the troops stationed in Laiyang have already set off today (17th) and will arrive in Yantai tomorrow. They will immediately board ships and leave Shandong. The problem of filling the defense of Jiaodong will have to wait until Liu's troops have completed their withdrawal before the provincial troops can arrange to fill the defense.

Liu Zhennian's 21st Division has been actively expanding in recent years, and its size is several times larger than that of a division, totaling nine infantry regiments, one cavalry regiment, one artillery regiment, one engineer battalion, one transport battalion, two reserve infantry regiments, and one company each of the military officer training corps, special service, and military music corps. In addition, there is a machinery repair shop, with a total number of 31,000 people. Now, they have been ordered to be transferred to eastern Zhejiang and are about to set off. He Yingqin, Minister of Military Administration, sent a telegram to Xiong Bin in Jinan today (17th), stating that Liu's troops are too numerous and do not conform to the central government's organization. Please inform Liu to quickly downsize according to the central government's regulations into a Class B division (i.e., each division has two brigades, and each brigade has three regiments). The central government had already ordered the abolition of the military officer training corps, which must be disbanded as soon as possible. Most of the soldiers under his command are from Jiaodong. They should be discharged in Jiaodong, retaining the strong and eliminating the weak, and actively downsize before boarding the ship to avoid the trouble of downsizing and transporting them back and forth after arriving in eastern Zhejiang. In the future, they will receive their salaries on a monthly basis and diligently train them to serve the country. Shortly after this telegram arrived, another telegram was received from He Yingqin, informing that he had received Liu Zhennian's telegram reporting the order of departure. Director Wang Jinglu also sent a cold telegram to Xiong, informing him that twelve ships had been hired to transport Liu Zhennian's troops. Because the tides in Yantai are rough, except for the ships berthed at the pier, the rest must anchor seventy miles outside the port at Grandma Mountain. All ships must leave to avoid prolonged anchoring and lack of coal and fresh water. Xian's telegram also reported that the Shengan Wheel had departed at [time], the Xinfeng Wheel had departed at [time], and the Shihe Wheel was not repaired and another ship must be hired to transport them. In addition, Fu Xingpei, sent by Zhang Xueliang to Yexian, also sent a telegram to Xiong reporting that order had been restored after arriving in Yexian. Soon after, there was another telegram reporting the order of departure of Liu's troops. Liu Zhennian himself telegraphed Xiong Bin from Laiyang, welcoming him to Yexian and stating that there was no definite date for his return to Yexian and that he would telegraph again after the date was set. As for the date of Xiong's departure to Yexian, it has been set for the 18th, and he will meet with Liu Zhennian in Yexian. (17th)

Japanese Ships Illegally Fishing in Our Territorial Waters 68

▲ Japanese Consul Ingeniously Claims it Was to Avoid Wind and Waves

Jinan Correspondence: Japanese fishing boats often openly fish in the territorial waters of Shandong Province. The Department of Industry had previously sent a letter to Nishi, the Japanese Consul in Jinan, requesting that he stop this. Recently, a letter was received from him with extremely clever wording, stating, "Respectfully, regarding the matter of Japanese fishing boats fishing near Sangdao Island in Huangxian County, I was instructed to find a way to stop it. I replied to your department on August 8th with the Hua Shi No. 6 official letter stating that the county is under the jurisdiction of the Zhifu Consul and I have informed the relevant authorities. Now, according to a letter from the Acting Consul of Zhifu, the ship belongs to the Kwantung Governor-General and is ordered to conduct investigations in the territorial waters. As for the fishing, it was not the [ship name] but the Hiruko Maru. According to the captain, the ship temporarily anchored in the territorial waters due to wind and waves, but the operation was actually outside the territorial waters and it is about to return home. At that time, I instructed them not to fish within Chinese territorial waters and the ship should comply with this. This is for your reference. Sincerely, Nishi Koichi, Japanese Consul to Shandong Department of Industry Director Wang Zaiji."

Wuxi 71

▲ County Party Committee Member Returns Home Safely: Yao Xinshun, a member of the Executive Committee of the Wuxi County Party Committee, went to Shanghai with his wife a month ago for some matters. After living there for only two days, he suddenly disappeared. Although he was searched for everywhere, there was no trace of him. His family was extremely anxious. A few days ago, there was suddenly a clue that Yao was in Shanghai. His family rushed to find him and he returned home safely the day before yesterday, but he was mentally exhausted and acted passively. He immediately telegraphed the Provincial Party Committee requesting his resignation. He received a reply yesterday, retaining him and granting him two weeks of leave.

▲ Water Police District Strictly Guarding Against Lake Bandits: The Water Police District No. 2 in Wuxi, given that the Taihu Lake bandits have been rampant all year round, and now that it is winter, the bandits are thinking of moving again, has ordered strict precautions. It has also ordered the Bao Su and Xun Ping ships to depart immediately to patrol the lake surface. It has also ordered the seventh team leader, Pei Xuan, to pay close attention to the mountains, cliffs, and reeds on the lake surface. Director Shen is scheduled to go to Dongting West Mountain and the two counties of Yixing and Liyang within days to inspect the situation.

▲ Three Fires Broke Out in the City and Countryside in One Day: In the monk's residence of the Puxian North Courtyard, next to the Xiongdi Photography Shop on Gongyuan Road in the city, a fire suddenly broke out at 11:30 PM on the 18th, causing a conflagration. The flames were so bright that they could not be approached. At that time, the abbot of the temple, Hongda, the monk Rongpei, and the old woman who cooked the incense and rice, were all awakened from their dreams and fled in panic, grabbing cotton quilts to avoid danger. Fortunately, the fire brigades of each section heard the alarm and rushed to the scene to put out the fire. After about an hour, the fire was extinguished, but three ordinary houses had been reduced to ashes. Also, a fire broke out in a pheasant nest of the Zhang family near the Second Branch Bureau outside Guangfu Gate at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, resulting in the burning of an empty house. Furthermore, a fire alarm was reported at the Dalong Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant in Xintangqiao, the Second District (Jingyun City), at 8:00 PM the day before yesterday. The fire brigades of Jiangxiqiao and Yangting successively drew water to extinguish the fire, resulting in losses of more than 1,000 yuan.

▲ Election Fraud Causing Disputes: During the re-election of the Township Chief and Supervisor in Dagang Township, outside Nanmen, on August 26th of this year, citizen Pu Shuying believed it to be illegal and immediately convened a township meeting, causing conflicts with Qiu Boying and others. The election was inconclusive. Afterwards, Pu filed a private prosecution with the Criminal Court of the County Court, accusing Qiu Boying of assault and accusing Qian Zhongliang, the Chief of the First District, of instigating assault. Qiu Boying also filed a complaint with the Procuratorate against Pu Shuying for disrupting the election, and Chief Qian also hired a lawyer to draft a counterclaim to the Criminal Court, requesting that Pu be prosecuted for false accusation. Yesterday was the date for the court hearing. At 5:00 PM, Judge Liang opened the court to interrogate. The defendants Pu Shuying, Qiu Boying, Qian Zhongliang, and the witnesses Xu Zonglian, Li Jianlie, Zhu Guangzu, Gu Ziwen, Wang Rongchun, and the defense lawyers Tang Ying and Deng Shuren were present. First, Pu Shuying was interrogated, stating that in August, because the villagers were dissatisfied with the illegal election, Qiu Boying assaulted him and Chief Qian incited the assault. He requested that they be punished according to the law. Next, Qiu Boying stated that the assault claimed by Pu was fabricated, and Qian also stated that Pu's accusation was completely false. After reviewing the statements, Judge Liang advised them to withdraw the private prosecution in court. Pu insisted on refusing, so the lawyers for both parties stood up to argue. After the debate, Judge Liang announced the end of the debate and set a date for sentencing on the 22nd of this month. The plaintiff, Pu Shuying, was released on bail and the others were ordered to return home.

▲ Appeal for the Levy of Donations for Ship Registration: The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau has recently sent personnel to Wuxi to organize a registration office. Every day, three or four people in plain clothes and suits hire small boats and intercept passing ships at the inner river checkpoints and old tax collection points in the north and south ponds near the city, claiming to be inspectors, ordering them to register and demanding a registration fee of 11.6 yuan, divided into numerous items such as licenses, measurements, and nationality registration. Even small ships cannot be exempted. However, ship owners believe that the original intention of the Maritime Affairs Bureau was not to collect donations, but to maintain maritime administration and protect foreign interests. Now that it has added various fees, the ships that have to pass through the customs to travel on the Yangtze River and sea already feel that it violates the original intention. How can it impose huge donations on the inner river ships? Therefore, they have requested the shipping industry association to assist them. The association believes that there may be regulations for ship registration, but precautions should be taken against malpractices at the beginning of implementation. Recently, the waterways have been unstable and ships have often encountered bandits and robberies on the way. After being robbed by treacherous people, they set up checkpoints and collect fees. Furthermore, the inner river sailing ships are small businesses, and the inner river steamships have already registered according to regulations. If they are forced to register again, they should issue an order to the ship owners to register themselves, and should not intercept them on the way for inspection. Therefore, the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the National Government Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Transportation, the Ministry of Industry, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the Department of Industry, and the Department of Construction, requesting assistance to abolish all ship registration offices everywhere.

It happened that Xiang Lusheng, the manager of Yuanda Village in the city, went to the Gao family for something. The woman asked to go with Xiang. Her parents-in-law reluctantly agreed. When Xiang arrived at the Wang family, he did not see the woman. He asked the family and they did not know. He went out to look for her and found her body in the well at the back door of the Wang residence. She had already died when she was pulled out.

Ministry of Education Announces Teaching and Self-Study Hours for Senior and Junior High Schools 79

Nanjing, 19th – The Ministry of Education has announced the weekly teaching and self-study hours for various subjects in senior and junior high schools. For senior high school, the total weekly teaching hours for all subjects are 34 hours each in the first, second, and third semesters, 33 hours in the fourth semester, and 31 hours each in the fifth and sixth semesters. The total weekly hours for extracurricular activities and on-campus self-study are 26 hours each in the second and third semesters, 27 hours in the fourth semester, and 29 hours each in the fifth and sixth semesters. For junior high school, the total weekly math hours are 5 hours each in the first, second, third, and fifth semesters, and 34 hours in the fourth and sixth semesters. The total weekly hours for extracurricular activities and on-campus self-study are 13 hours each in the first, second, third, and fifth semesters, and 14 hours in the fourth and sixth semesters.

New Minister of Education, Weng Wenhao, Firmly Declines 81

Discussing the Difficulties and Challenges in the Education Sector

Requests Song Ziwen to Appoint Someone Else

Beiping Special Dispatch – The new Minister of Education, Weng Wenhao, is still in Beiping, holding the position of Director of the Geological Survey Institute. He has repeatedly declined the position of Minister, but the Central Government has not approved it. Today (16th), it was widely rumored in Beiping and Tianjin that Weng had agreed to take the position of Minister and would go to the capital soon to take office. The reporter went to Weng's private residence to inquire about the truth. He agreed to be interviewed, and the key points of the conversation are recorded below:

▲ Weng Wenhao stated that his previous trip to Nanjing was not specifically to resign from the position of Minister of Education, but he took the opportunity to make this request. Before returning to Beiping, he had discussed it with the President of the Executive Yuan, Song Ziwen. Today, President Song sent a telegram again asking him to take the position of Minister of Education, but he still firmly declined. The rumor that he would go to the capital to take office is not true. He is very interested in studying geology and is unwilling to take on educational administrative affairs. In the past, the Ministry of Education appointed him as the President of Tsinghua University, but he also declined. This proves that he is unwilling to handle educational administration. Based on this principle, he resolutely declines the position of Minister. The Ministry of Education is still temporarily headed by Minister Zhu (Jiahua), with the assistance of Vice Ministers Duan (Xipeng) and Qian (Changzhao). Since he is unwilling to do it, he has already sent a telegram to President Song, asking him to appoint someone else. He believes that the Ministry of Education has many difficult problems. First, the most difficult problem is funding. There is a shortage of educational funding nationwide, and it is difficult to handle the annual increase in school classes, and there is no way to expand. For example, the Beiping University Medical College has been changed to a six-year system, but the funding for the reform has not been secured. The Russian-French Law College has been reorganized into a Business College, but the funding for expanding the facilities has not been allocated. Other universities have similar situations. Second, the situation in the education sector is complicated. Recently, there have been rumors of changes in the organization of Normal Universities. He thinks that this matter may not be implemented. The various outstanding cases of Beiping University and the reorganization of Normal University have not been considered yet because he is unwilling to head the Ministry of Education (Weng smiled at the reporter when he said this). Chairman Jiang (Zhongzheng) is very concerned about education, but he is currently traveling around and may not have time to take care of the selection of the Minister of Education. He originally wanted to go to the capital, but to avoid suspicion, he will not go now. The rumor that he will be appointed as the Minister of Education after the Third Plenary Session is not true. If the Third Plenary Session announces that he is the Minister, he will firmly decline.

▲ Telegram to Song Ziwen: Mr. Weng received a telegram from Song Ziwen, the acting President of the Executive Yuan, today, urging him to stay. He personally drafted a reply telegram on the same day, requesting that someone else be appointed. The original telegram is recorded below: "To His Excellency Song Ziwen, President of the Executive Yuan, Nanjing: I have earnestly stated before that I am truly incapable and that it is difficult to leave the geological work suddenly. Please consider my foolishness and approve it, and appoint someone else to avoid a vacancy. Weng Wenhao, respectfully, November 16th."

Representatives of Elementary Schools in Beiping Postpone Going South 83

Beiping, 19th – Due to lack of travel funds, the trip south by the representatives of elementary schools has been postponed.

Ministry of Education Promulgates Curriculum Standards for Kindergartens and Elementary Schools (3) 84

(6) Quiet Time

I. Objectives: (A) Directly satisfying mental health; (B) Indirectly increasing the efficiency of mental activities.

II. Content: (A) Silence: Following the Montessori method, timed silences are held. After hearing a certain sound signal (either a bell or a certain tone), everyone must sit upright. The teacher guides the child on duty to take the silence sign (gray with black letters) and put it next to the blackboard, while observing whether there are any children who are not silent. After everyone is quiet, everyone is told to close their eyes. At this time, (a) either clasp hands and droop their heads for support and rest; (b) or lean on the table and lie down; (c) or sleep on the table. The teacher retreats to a corner. After two or three minutes, another sound signal is made to make everyone look up. The sound signal can also be changed after a month or two, sometimes with a playful meaning. The time can be gradually increased. For example, after the teacher leaves the room and everyone is quiet, she goes to another room and calls a child's name in a pleasant voice after two or three minutes. The child who is called will run to her arms like a flying swallow. Then, another child's name is called, and so on until everyone has left. This game can be called "Flying Swallows Returning to Their Nests." Beforehand, the children can be told that quiet time in the Montessori kindergarten is held more than once a day, with around 10 o'clock (after eating snacks for those who eat snacks) being the most suitable. (B) Quiet Resting: For those who have a full-day system, it is best to prepare bedding for each child. After lunch, they retire for quiet resting. Small children should sleep for more than two hours, and older children should sleep for one and a half hours. Others should not be disturbed when they wake up. (Note: New-style kindergartens in England pay great attention to this point.)

(7) Snacks

I. Objectives: (A) Meeting Needs: Children have small appetites, so the distance between eating times must be short. From breakfast to noon, there are five hours, and a small amount of biscuits and other snacks are needed in between to satisfy hunger. (B) Practicing proper etiquette during eating. (C) Developing proper hygiene habits during eating. (D) Developing the habit of cherishing food.

II. Content: Around 10:00 every morning, each child eats appropriate food (yams, biscuits, etc.) and drinks a cup of boiled water (those with ample funds can use milk instead of water or eat a small amount of fruit).

III. Key Points of Educational Methods

(1) The various activities listed above (music, games, stories and nursery rhymes, social nature, work, etc.) should be integrated into one when actually implemented, without so-called subjects. The method of integrating into one should be based on a kind of needed material (seasonal, such as the tree planting festival in March, the National Day in October, the red leaves in autumn, the white snow in winter, etc., discovered in the environment, such as making a birthday for a doll, burying a dead beneficial bird publicly, holding a parents' meeting, etc.) as the center of the operation for a day or two or three days. All activities are inseparable from the scope of this center.

(2) The time that young children spend in the kindergarten every day is about six hours for the whole day. Kindergartens with special circumstances in the city can use a half-day system, about three hours every morning. In addition to scheduled snacks, quiet rest, and stopping work for lunch and scheduled quiet rest in the whole-day system, various activities should not be rigidly divided into sections (such as what kind of homework should be taught every hour). However, the teacher should have a plan in mind, leading the children to do light activities after heavy work, leading the children to do outdoor exercises after working at the table, and may intersperse a few minutes of rest after a certain activity to adjust the children's physical and mental health.

(3) Various homework can be done by children freely from their own interests, but group homework should also be done once a day. The teacher uses suggestive methods to attract children to operate together. If a small number of children do not want to participate in group homework, there is no need to force them.

(4) Stories, games, music, society and nature can mostly be guided by the teacher to implement group homework, while work should mostly be done by children individually, with individual guidance from the teacher. These activities can divide all homework into several items (such as drawing, cutting and pasting, building blocks, etc.) for children to cooperate in groups and divide the work, but attention should be paid to two things: First, grouping two or three people into a group to cooperate in one thing is the most effective. Second, children often do not finish this thing and then go to do that thing, or give up halfway, or do it perfunctorily. The teacher should train them to have a sense of responsibility. The training method can be to use symbols to show which ones can be completed and give them reward symbols, otherwise give them warning symbols, or express goodwill to those who have completed them and indifference to those who have not completed them.

(5) The teacher should be fully prepared to avoid temporary difficulties. The matters to be prepared should be determined according to the trend of children's activities. For example, before the National Day commemoration activity, the teacher should collect materials and prepare skills for how many problems and facts are expected to occur in the children's National Day commemoration activity, so as to cope with them.

(6) The materials presented by the teacher to guide children's activities and the methods of guiding children's activities, as well as all progress, must consider children's psychology and be in line with children's experiences.

(7) The materials used in early childhood education are not empty words, but real objects and facts that can be seen and touched daily, or at least imagined. The places used in early childhood education are not limited to indoors, but must take outdoor nature, family, village, city, industry and commerce as the best places for activities.

(8) Kindergarten design teaching must pay attention to the following points: First, discover design topics from children's free activities. For example, a child plants cabbage in the sandbox. After the teacher discovers it, he can gather many children to design planting vegetables. This is a good opportunity in design teaching and should be used. Second, all activities that should be in the design should have long considered the children's ability to remove the parts that children cannot do or cannot do well to avoid children abandoning because they cannot do or being frustrated because of failure in the middle. Third, the design materials should be easy to achieve the purpose and easy to get results. In a design, it must be divided into many small paragraphs, each small paragraph has a small purpose and can get a small result, then children will do it according to it, and it will naturally be interested to reach the purpose and get results and be willing to work hard. If the whole design is done halfway and the interest of most children has shifted, then the teacher can also put down this design and then engage in the design where the interest of most children lies, and then find a way to continue when the appropriate time comes.

(9) The teacher is the helmsman in the children's activities, and he must make the children follow his trend to proceed. Before reaching the goal, do not change the purpose, and the suggestions issued should also be consistent and not mixed. When the children have reacted but have not reached completion, there must be no new suggestions.

(10) The teacher is the final judge. The children's problems should be solved by the children themselves. Only when the children really cannot solve it can the teacher inspire and guide them from the side.

(11) The teacher should use rewards to encourage children's interest in certain homework. Rewards for young children are most effective with verbal and toy gifts, followed by symbol rewards. The rewards should pay attention to: First, rewards should not be used frequently, otherwise they will be abused and lose their effectiveness. Second, it is of course right to reward those who excel in the crowd, but also to reward individuals who have made sudden progress in comparison before and after.

(12) There are several skills that should be made proficient by children by using the "practice" method. The conditions that must be taken care of in practice are as follows: First, the time should be short to maintain children's interest and attention in practice. Second, the number of times should be in line with the principle of distributed practice (at the beginning, practice quickly in a certain short time every day, and then practice intermittently after being familiar with it, and only stop after being proficient). Third, the materials used for practice must be estimated to have real value, and do not waste effort if it is not necessary to practice. Fourth, the method of practice must be checked to see if it is the most excellent, and it is certain that it will be laborious and useless if the method is misused (for example, practicing abstract symbols instead of using real objects). Fifth, when practicing, not only should we pay attention to the children's performance, but also to whether the methods used by the children are appropriate or not. If they are inappropriate, they must be corrected at any time.

(13) A "physical examination" should be held every six months, a "height and weight examination" should be held every month, and a "health and cleanliness examination" should be held every day (the details are in the curriculum standards for elementary school hygiene and other subjects). The teacher should try to remedy the physical defects and various diseases of the children. The teacher should not only have the intelligence of a mother and teacher, but also have the skills of a nurse and the common sense of treating diseases.

(14) The teacher should pay attention to the children's body, temperament, hobbies, as well as family and environment. It is best to prepare a small booklet to record the observations as materials for research and teaching.

(15) The teacher should often go to the children's homes or invite parents to the kindergarten to try to connect feelings and promote the methods of early childhood education and family education.

(16) In addition to using outdoor nature and society, kindergartens should equip everything according to the following standards: First, it must conform to the national character of our country. The national character of our country is sincerity, perseverance, and different from Europe, America, and Japan. The equipment of kindergartens does not need to be too gorgeous, but must pay attention to solidity. It does not need to take too many foreign styles and imported goods, but must be as Chinese as possible. Second, it must conform to the local social situation. Our country has a vast territory, and the social situations of cities, villages, south, north soil, rich areas, and barren areas are different. The equipment of kindergartens should take more common items in the local area and not be separated from the actual situation of the society. Third, it must meet the needs of children. It is necessary to consider the children's physiological condition, psychological state, and living situation and equip them according to their needs. (A) The quantity should not be too simple, and it is expected to be enough. (B) The quality should be convenient for children to apply. Fourth, it must not violate the meaning of education. On the positive side, it should be (A) able to develop children's creativity and stimulate children's imagination; (B) can be used by children themselves and can be installed or disassembled by themselves; (C) can arouse children's interest and aesthetic sense; (D) can arouse children's emotions; (E) can develop children's intelligence; (F) is beneficial to children's body. On the negative side, it should be (A) Unhygienic ones are not taken. (B) Dangerous ones are not taken. (C) Children are not interested in them. (D) Ones that damage the beauty are not taken. Fifth, it is necessary to use waste materials, natural materials and daily necessities. Waste materials such as old books, old newspapers, rags, useless glass pieces, glass bottles, cloth pieces, broken bowls, natural materials such as fruit pits, leaves, petals, seeds, clam shells, shells, bird feathers, pebbles, daily necessities such as soap, candles, etc. can be used to make educational supplies, decorations, and homework materials, etc. This not only saves money, but also inspires children's creativity.

Jiangsu Province's Circular Prohibiting Students from Fundraising 86

Zhou Fohai, the Director of the Jiangsu Education Bureau, in view of the fact that students often engage in fundraising activities, which wastes their studies and causes social misunderstandings and numerous malpractices, which has a profound impact on the future of education, specially issued a circular to all levels of schools under his jurisdiction to prohibit them. He also proposed that the provincial government conference issue a circular to all counties to announce the prohibition. It has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The original order is recorded below:

When the Director of this Bureau attended the meeting of primary school principals in Wuxian County this month on the 14th, he was surprised to hear that students in public and private middle schools in Wuxian County had stopped classes to go out and fundraise. He was deeply surprised. He then patrolled the city and saw male and female students all over the streets and alleys, either blocking vehicles and cutting off traffic, or breaking into people's homes and destroying tranquility to fundraise. If fundraising was not successful, they would often utter bad words, causing passers-by to look at them, society to be uneasy, the people to be angry and resentful, and the market to be suspicious. What is even more painful is that young girls lingered on the streets, and gangsters took the opportunity to make fun of them and be frivolous. The dignity of the school was swept away, and social ethics were destroyed. All kinds of situations were witnessed by the Director of this Bureau. The loss of stopping classes and the gains of fundraising are obviously very different. Sacrificing the precious time of thousands of students to gain a drop of fundraising is already a loss. Moreover, there are numerous malpractices and people are talking about it. It is even more heart-wrenching. What is the purpose of the principals? They only rely on the resolutions of student groups to let them stop classes freely without discouraging them, which is a dereliction of duty. If this trend is not corrected quickly, it will have a profound impact on the future of education. This special circular is issued to all principals, requesting them to repeatedly explain the pros and cons of stopping classes and fundraising to the students and to strictly prohibit them. Do not have any worries or be perfunctory. The Director of this Bureau will never sit idly by and watch the young people who are the future masters of the country indulge in the false name of patriotism, waste their own studies, ruin their social faith, and move towards suicide. In addition to proposing that the provincial government conference issue a circular to all counties to announce the prohibition, if there are any such incidents, they should be forcibly dispersed with real force. In addition to separate orders, this urgent order is issued to the directors of the bureaus, requesting them to forward it to all schools under their jurisdiction for compliance.

Business and Medical Colleges Still Belong to Zhongda Movement 87

▲ Alumni Associations of Graduates from Central University, Dongda University, and Nanga University Host Journalists

Nanjing, 19th – On the afternoon of the 9th, the General Association of Alumni of Graduates from Central University, Dongda University, and Nanga University hosted reporters to request the government to restore the Business and Medical Colleges. Fu Yulin and Xiao Yanbin successively reported the reasons for requesting the government to restore the colleges: 1. To complete the organization of the National University; 2. After the Business and Medical Colleges are independent, they will deprive the entire funding of Central University and increase the burden on students, hindering the advancement of poor children; 3. The Business and Medical Colleges are located in Shanghai, and the transportation between Shanghai and Nanjing is convenient, so there is no difficulty in management; 4. The pre-medical course is attached to the College of Science. After the separation, these students have nowhere to go, and the facilities of the College of Science are better and research is more convenient. Finally, the alumni who have graduated and are still in school unanimously advocate the restoration of the colleges and will not stop until the goal is achieved. The first step is to arouse the sympathy of the public opinion circles, the second step is to ask the party and state elders for assistance, and the third step is to petition the Third Plenary Session.

Kwang Hua Wins the Fourteen Middle School Cross-Country Championship 97

▲ First Place Individual, Da Xia’s Chen Zhiyuan, Time 17 Minutes, 54.6 Seconds

The Middle School Athletic Advancement Association of Shanghai held the middle school cross-country competition yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the Kwang Hua Middle School attached to the university on the Great Western Road. Fourteen schools registered to participate. McLaren Middle School was absent due to circumstances, so thirteen schools with a total of sixty-five participants actually attended. Kwang Hua Middle School attached to the university won the championship with eighteen points. Pudong came in second, and Qingxin came in third. The first place individual was Chen Zhiyuan from Da Xia. Liu Chongli from Kwang Hua came in second by a narrow margin. Zhan Yiji from Kwang Hua came in third with a time of seventeen minutes, fifty-four and six-tenths seconds. It is truly remarkable that middle school students can run such a time in the three-and-a-half mile race. Recalling the cross-country race held by Jiangnan University at Kwang Hua in 1928, the best time was eighteen minutes and forty-four seconds by Wang Zishao of Kwang Hua. The fact that middle school students can now surpass the achievements of university students in the same course demonstrates the hard work and effective promotion of practice in various schools in recent years. The following is a brief description of the competition at that time.

▲Struggling Along the Way

At exactly 2:00 PM, the athletes from various schools eagerly entered the field in a light breeze and drizzle. After Chen Yuze, the starter, briefly explained the rules, he fired the starting gun. The participants formed a long line, like a snake, along the route. From the Great Western Road through Avenue Foch and Route Hobbema, veteran and new competitors were scattered. When they reached Lincoln Avenue, Liu Chongli from Kwang Hua was leading the pack, running swiftly. Following Liu were Chen Zhiyuan from Da Xia and Zhan Yiji from Kwang Hua. The others also chased hard with all their strength. As they approached the finish line, Chen and Liu gritted their teeth, fighting for the lead, but Chen Zhiyuan from Da Xia ultimately surpassed Liu Chongli by a shoulder's length to take first place. All sixty others also reached the finish line within twenty-five minutes, demonstrating a commendable spirit of perseverance.

▲Grand Award Ceremony

After the race, the athletes from all the schools gathered in the Kwang Hua assembly hall, enjoying tea and refreshments in a lively and grand atmosphere. Then, Mr. Zheng Xigu, the chairman of the Middle School Athletic Advancement Association, took the stage to give a speech, encouraging the athletes to save the country through physical education. He also introduced Mr. Liao Maoru to present the awards. After Mr. Liao announced the results of the competition, the audience erupted in applause and congratulated each other. Prizes were awarded to the top five teams and the top ten individuals. The results are listed below.

Western Football League First Division: Kiangnan Defeated by Westerners Police 100

│Result: 2-5│

▲Lost Momentum in the First Half...0-3

▲Showed Their Skills in the Second Half...2-2

Kiangnan has lost, defeated by the strong team, Westerners Police. The Westerners Police are not as strong as in previous years, yet Kiangnan was defeated, which shows their relative strength. Some say that Kiangnan’s players have an indomitable spirit, and that yesterday’s defeat may prove to be an effective stimulant. We will wait and see. Yesterday was a match in the Westerners Association First Division League. Westerners Police won with a score of 5-2. The two teams’ lineups were as follows:

Westerners Police Team Lineup 101

Wei Jinsheng

Xiao De, He Lei, De Fei

Aitman, Gaxu, Poke

Turner, Weisiwu, Jack

Okley

Kiangnan Team Lineup 102

Liu Zukan

Gu Shangxiang, Liang Shutang, Luo Haiguang

Xie Quanhe, Xu Yahui, Chen Zhenhe

Jiang Shanjing, Zhuang Shihong, Chen Zhenhe

Mei Hongbao

▲The Momentum Was Impressive When They Took the Field 103

Kiangnan kicked off, circling the opponent's mid-field. Their momentum was formidable. Chen Zhenhe headed the ball to the left, and Liu Zukan met it in the center. The situation became tense. Goalkeeper Aitman caught the ball with both hands, averting the danger. Xu Yahui intercepted halfway and led the attack again, forcing a corner kick, but ultimately without success. Although Kiangnan held the advantage, their forwards did not coordinate well, often missing opportunities at crucial moments. Chen Zhenhe was left to assist alone, making it difficult to achieve any special results.

▲The Defense Was Breached Repeatedly Within Ten Minutes 104

Unfortunately, Zhuang Shihong injured his ankle but continued to play, though his agility was reduced. The opposing players invaded everywhere. Right inside forward Jack scored with a long shot from about thirty yards from the goal. A good defender might have prevented this. The second goal was scored by center-back Gaxu from a free kick, precisely and beautifully into the top left corner, as if his foot had eyes. Okley scored the third goal after Wei Jinsheng kicked a corner kick. Amidst a crowd of players, one strike was all it took. Kiangnan was not weak. After each goal conceded, they launched a fierce counterattack, but the result was always zero because they could not tighten up in time. In the first half, they lost momentum and conceded three goals.

Morale Boosted After the Break 105

After the break, the two armies realigned and fought again. Kiangnan returned to their original form, striving to achieve. Xu Yahui had a chance with a penalty kick, heading straight for the enemy's goal. Chen Zhenxiang rushed forward, but the ball had already turned back, and Chen was offside. At that time, Kiangnan was on the attack, and Okley advanced swiftly on the flank. Jiang and Gu resisted poorly, and the ball went to the center, where new player Poke took advantage and scored, taking a 4-0 lead. Kiangnan launched another attack. Liu Zukan kicked a corner kick. After three or four passes, it hit an enemy's arm. Chen Zhenhe himself scored the penalty kick. He kicked with force, but the goalkeeper caught it. The whistle blew, saying that the kick had to be taken again because a Westerners Police inside back had entered the penalty area at the same time as Chen, which was against the rules. The second time, Chen kicked the ball just inside the post, and the score was opened. Kiangnan's morale was boosted. Liu picked up the ball and passed to the goalkeeper, who caught it. Chen Zhenhe swooped down like a heavenly general, his body colliding with the goalkeeper. Chen touched the ball in the air with his foot. Chen's bravery and divine power were universally praised.

▲Ambushed Again Before the End 106

Kiangnan scored two goals in a row, and hope suddenly arose. Liu had two more chances, but his measures were inappropriate, otherwise, another situation could have occurred. After thirty minutes, He Lei sent a long ball, and Poke happened to be there, heading it into the goal. The result was 5-2. Kiangnan's hope of winning was dashed. After that, there was nothing but back and forth play, without any further scores. Kiangnan ultimately lost 2-5. The referee was Reynolds.

East Asia's forwards advanced step by step. The score was eventually surpassed from a tie to a 32-29 lead. East Asia turned defeat into victory by 3 points. Kiangnan suffered a crushing defeat by three points.
