Letters to the Editor 174

To the Esteemed Editor, Greetings. I am writing in astonishment after reading the news "All Shanghai Students to Meet Tomorrow" in your newspaper on the 19th. It states that all Shanghai students of all ages and various cultural groups are scheduled to meet at our school at 9:00 AM on the 20th. Our school was not informed of this matter beforehand. All the classrooms in our school are very small and cannot accommodate so many people gathering. Furthermore, our school has not set up an office for this meeting. Therefore, I am writing to request a correction, hoping you will publish it in the local news section to avoid misunderstandings from the outside world. With best wishes, Daxia University Admissions Office, November 19th.

To the Reporter, Greetings. Today, your newspaper published a news item in the local news section titled "All Shanghai Students to Meet Tomorrow," which stated that the preparatory committee for the joint association of all Shanghai students supporting the Northeastern Volunteer Army against the Lytton Commission's report had appointed Chen Bin as an honorary member of the association and that he would attend and give a speech. In fact, the association did not obtain Chen Bin's consent for this matter and had already received a polite refusal in a letter the day before. I am writing to request a correction. With best wishes, Chen Bin, November 19th.

Greetings. I have read the news published in your newspaper about the strike and disturbances of workers at the China General Edison Company. The facts are slightly inconsistent. Here are the facts of the matter: (1) Since February, the workers of our union have requested the company to improve their living and treatment. More than half a year has passed, and the management has not sincerely adopted any measures. Even after repeated mediation by party and government organs, there has been no result, leading to widespread indignation and a work slowdown. (2) After the streetcar key was lost in the morning, the workers seized the opportunity to spontaneously slow down work. Upon learning of this, the directors of our union immediately rushed to the company to persuade the public to restore traffic and await mediation, but to no avail. Subsequently, representatives of party and government organs held a meeting, but there was still no solution. (3) After implementing the slowdown, the workers collectively demanded that Lu, the company manager, immediately agree to the salary increase conditions. Unexpectedly, at around 3:00 PM, because the workers were tired of standing, they pushed out a streetcar to use as a chair. For some unknown reason, gunshots suddenly rang out, causing chaos. As a result, workers Wang A-si and Li Fugen were seriously injured on the spot, and their lives are in danger. More than a dozen others were slightly injured and have all been sent to Renji Shanghai Hospital, etc., for treatment. Your newspaper's report that the injuries were caused by a bomb is inaccurate. Please correct it according to this letter to avoid misunderstandings. To the Editor of Shen Bao, from the Shanghai First District Water and Electricity Industry Workers' Union, November 19, 1932.

Free Talk

The Evolution of Society 175

— Bi

│All Depends on Dissatisfaction│

Coming out of school, the place to eat is still not settled, and needing three copper coins for pocket money requires digging into the pockets of one's parents. At that time, the plan was just to find a boss and receive a monthly salary of ten dollars, which would be very satisfying. After waiting for a year and a half, relying on the spirits of one's ancestors in heaven, one actually found a job with a monthly salary of thirty dollars, which was such a joyful thing. But at the end of the month, seeing other people's colorful banknotes, stacked one on top of another, going into their pockets, while oneself had worked hard for a month but only had three thin bills, one couldn't swallow this feeling. Therefore, one had to ask for help from relatives and friends to seek better employment. After the eating problem was solved, the first major problem was to plan how to find a satisfactory wife. With this thought, one felt that other people were staying together in pairs, and after work they returned to their residence, the two small mouths talked and laughed, and on weekends and holidays, they cooked a few dishes to eat, which was so interesting. Without a wife, after work one returned to the residence alone, and at mealtime, one still had to go to a restaurant, and weekends and holidays were even more boring. Therefore, one didn't choose what to eat and just married a wife to try it out. But after a year of marriage, an ignorant child was born with a loud cry. At that time, half of the wife's love was taken away by the child. After work, one returned to the residence, the teacup was on the chair, and diapers were scattered all over the floor. Everything felt unpleasant. Therefore, one had to look for other thoughts outside, seeking spiritual comfort.

Once the rice bowl was settled and the sexual troubles were resolved, one again envied those who rode in cars and lived in Western-style houses. Being the same person, why did others live in Western-style houses while I lived in a pavilion building; why did others ride in cars while I limped on the road every day? So, spend ten dollars to buy a champagne, and rely on the spirits of one's ancestors in heaven, and win one or two hundred thousand silver dollars, and all the clothing, food, housing, and transportation problems are solved. But if one or two hundred thousand silver dollars really came into hand, would one no longer have any extravagant hopes? I cannot guarantee that.

It is said that society evolves in this way.

Madame Pawley's Clever Escape from the Bandit's Den 176

— Ye Xinfo

│Deeply Understood the Thoughts and Weaknesses of the Chinese│

The case of British Mrs. Muriel Pawley being trapped in the bandit's den in Niuzhuang was the most sensational kidnapping case in recent years. Negotiations approached last month, and she was released. Yesterday, I met a Western friend, Mr. "Hude," who, when discussing the Pawley case, said that if Pawley and others (also Mr. Charles Corran) had not cleverly used their wits, they might have been killed. While detained in the bandit's den, although the food and drink were unclean, they were treated relatively well. However, they were threatened in every possible way, and the bandits often pretended to damage their bodies to scare them. The bandit leader, when in high spirits, even cut off one of her ears and minced it into meat paste. Mrs. Pawley not only spoke Chinese very fluently but also deeply understood the thoughts and weaknesses of the Chinese. Relying on this line of thought, she made constant efforts day and night and finally came up with a solution. She mustered her courage and told the bandit leader: "If we are killed, our ghosts will haunt you day and night, making sure you never have a peaceful day. Even worse, we will turn your ancestors and your descendants into turtles." While speaking, she wailed and cried, with extreme sorrow, and pretended to strike herself to commit suicide. The delicate cries of a weak woman were even more effective than the military force of a country. The bandits, seeing this situation, were moved and whispered to each other, greatly reducing the ransom. Within a few days, the negotiations were settled, and they went to redeem and release them without any difficulty.

Why Are You Afraid of Your Wife? 177

— Yan Chunfan

│The Cause of the Three Stages│

Being afraid of one's wife is not a talent unique to China; I am afraid that there are many in Europe and America as well. Why are you afraid of your wife? There are three stages of reasons, which I will record below:

Love; it is always good for husband and wife to be loving. The husband, in order to maintain the love between the two, complies with his wife in every way, as long as he can win her heart and avoid the inconvenience of quarreling.

Respect; When she sees that her husband can always be considerate of her feelings, she becomes even more spoiled! To avoid cracks in love, the man compromises. At this point, he has entered the stage of "respect."

Awe; Having entered the third stage, no matter how capable you are of killing thieves for thousands of miles, you cannot subdue her because rigidity cannot overcome softness. For example, a steel knife chopping soft silk cotton, no matter how much effort you use, you cannot cut it. Tang Liuru said: "Why be afraid of the ways of heaven, which are vague and distant? Why fear the ways of the earth, which are dark and obscure? What is to be feared is the person who is always watching over you!" The reader may ask if there is a way not to be afraid? I say there is, but I have to keep three parts of the secret.

Looking Down on People 178

— Shen Zhenyue

│Because of Class Inequality│

A blind person looks down on people because he cannot see them.

A bright-eyed person looking down on people is very surprising and also very painful?

A person from the city looks down on people when they go to the countryside, and a person wearing a long gown looks down on people in the home of a person wearing short clothes.

A rich person looks down on people when they go to the poor home of a person without money.

Rich people can freely insult poor people, and poor people dare not resist. Sometimes poor people criticize the wrongs of the rich, and the rich will rise up to resist with full force. This is also a scene of looking down on people, probably because of class inequality, which leads to this kind of looking down on people, the so-called "acting as if something is important," which is an award given to a group of people who look down on others?

How can we talk about justice in a society where people look down on others like this? How can we talk about equality?

Therefore, people who look down on others like this are the criminals who destroy justice and equality?

People who cherish equality will not destroy justice. People who destroy justice will definitely destroy public reason first. To protect justice and protect equality, we should overthrow those who violate justice by looking down on others!

However, the person wearing a long gown and the person wearing short clothes are the same person, and the person with money and the person without money are also the same person, so we should not look down on the poor. I really hope that the thought of looking down on people will disappear immediately.

Crossroads of Death 19 179

— Fan Yanqiao

Mu Liang said, "I don't feel particularly uncomfortable. After all, Shanghai is a big place, and you can spread out. If you get tired of staying at home, you can go outside to relax. Always being cooped up in a pigeon coop isn't the same thing." The young mistress of the Han family became impatient and first hummed a "hmph" from her nostrils, followed by, "It's not like you men. Once you go out, it's like a bird leaving its cage and never wanting to return. What interest do we women have unless we're watching a play, going to a restaurant, or strolling around an amusement park? It's lonely and bleak." Mu Liang plastered his face with a smile and said, "Don't complain. Tomorrow, I'll accompany you to go around." The young mistress of the Han family still said weakly, "Do you have time? I don't believe it." Mu Liang said lazily, "These past few days have been extremely tiring. We're used to Suzhou and can't stay up late. When it gets bright, how can we still sleep? If we keep playing, we'll get sick soon."

The young mistress of the Han family deliberately teased him, "Would you be tired if you had a woman accompanying you?"

Mu Liang said:

"Do you know what kind of fun we're having?"

"Who knows!" The young mistress of the Han family didn't have any smile on her face and said lightly, "It's just one hundred and eighty-one, a small garden, or the Eight Immortals Bridge."

"No! No!" We go dancing. Dancing is more interesting than gambling or prostitution. It's a pity that it's too late and too tiring." "Buy one and dance at home. It'll be comfortable and free," said the young mistress of the Han family, and then burst into laughter. Who knew that these words would strike Mu Liang's heart. Not long ago, he chased away a concubine, and now he wants to get another one, which would inevitably be ridiculed by her. Although he was sure that she had no ability to stop him, the more docile she was, the more embarrassed he was to hide it from her. Moreover, during a time of national crisis, during a time of refuge, it was even more embarrassing to talk about this matter. It was rare for her to bring it up first, so he had an opportunity. Therefore, he was very excited, and his two ambitious eyes were filled with smiles, staring brightly at the young mistress of the Han family and saying:

"Shanghai women are difficult to handle. Do you think it's as easy as when I was getting Ai Gu?"

"Nothing is difficult in the world if you put your heart into it."

"There's a dancer in the dance hall who's really good. A round face, plump and tender, like a freshly ripe jade dew honey peach. Her graceful figure is more flexible than a water snake. People say that a modern woman's butt is 'four nothings,' but I say her whole body is 'four nothings.' Even her words are elastic. People say that a woman's two eyes are electric, but I say her thirty-six thousand pores are all electric..."

Bullish American Cotton Ends, Continues Weakness 188

Yesterday, American cotton was firm initially due to buying by traders, but then weakened due to profit-taking and hedging in the South. Futures fell by 5 to 7 points, and spot prices fell by 5 points. English cotton futures fell by 1-2 points, and spot prices remained unchanged. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by 4 points. Indian cotton was firm initially due to buying by Japanese traders, but then softened due to rising exchange rates. Future of American Cotton Depends on War Debt Issues 189

New York, 18th: A report on the cotton market for the week states that raw cotton prices fell last week due to thin supply and the characteristic roll-over of December futures. Brokers connected to Japanese traders have been buying. European demand has shifted into a decline. Most are awaiting developments in the war debt issue. The weather has turned cold, delaying cotton harvests in the northern and northwestern cotton belts. However, in general, this year's cotton harvest is mostly complete, except for a small portion. According to the U.S. Cotton Office, if the current favorable weather continues, there may be a slight increase in the Texas harvest. The total harvest for the entire cotton belt this season is estimated to be 12 million bales. Attached is a summary of American cotton statistics for the weekend (in thousands of bales):

Grain and Rice Market Trends Slightly Firmer 191

▲ In South Shanghai Yesterday, Over a Dozen Inland Boats Arrived

In the morning, there was a large number of people at the market, and the shops slightly increased their inventories. As a result, Suzhou-Tongxiang goods rose by 2.5 jiao, and early and late rice each increased by 1 jiao. Foreign Dujian rice was sold as soon as it arrived, and the opening price was set.

▲ In Xinzha Yesterday, Thirteen or Fourteen Boats Arrived on the West Road

The urban and rural sales market saw activity, and Kunshan rice suddenly rose by 2 jiao. Bo rice merchants slightly moved, and prices rose by 1.5 jiao. Tongbian rice changed subtly, neither good nor bad. The total daily opening volume was around 4,000 dan.

Lively Sales of Ke Xian Rice in the South 192

│ │Quanzhou Continues to Actively Purchase... Supply Arrives Continuously│ │

Yesterday, the foreign rice market remained flat and soft. Local merchants were generally uninterested. Later, Chen Saigon rice of 700 bales was purchased from this street at a price of only 8 yuan. The rice quality was slightly better than the previous shipment, but the price was the same. The market outlook was even softer. Ke Xian rice continued to arrive, and more was being loaded for shipment. Inventories were gradually increasing. The market was initially watching for a soft trend, but yesterday, southern merchants showed great interest in purchasing, resulting in a total turnover of around 4,000. In addition to the Fuzhou merchants purchasing nearly 1,000 bales, new Quanzhou merchants arrived in the market to inquire and immediately purchased it. About 3,000 bales of Gan and Xiang Xian rice were sold, allowing the market to stand firm.

Flour Market Enters a Firm Trend in the Afternoon 193

After the flour market opened yesterday morning, the market for each month showed an initial flat and then stable trend. Because the price of foreign wheat fell by another one or two jiao, the market atmosphere was flat at the beginning. However, after the second session, because there were very few sales, guest merchants had transactions, and floating shorts were also gradually covered. Therefore, the market rebounded and became firm. Until the afternoon market opened, the near-term months were because the Yingkou merchants had quite a lot of transactions, and Fufeng's short-covering of this month was presumably due to the need for spot goods and had not stopped, so the market sentiment recovered. As for the distant months, it was rumored that Australian wheat prices had been set, and due to exchange rate factors, the prices were called up by two or three points, but there were still few problems with setting orders. Only outsiders inevitably saw the price set. As a result, this month rose by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, December rose by 2 fen, January rose by 1 fen, February rose by 1.25 fen, March rose by 0.7 fen, and April rose by 1 fen.

Near-Term Wheat Rises by 3 Fen 194

│Far-Month Trends Flat Due to Foreign Wheat│

After the wheat futures market opened yesterday morning and afternoon, the market for each month showed a near-stable and far-flat trend. This month, because the supply of spot wheat was limited and the factory's appetite was still good, and there were not many chips in the exchange, the market was easily shaken as soon as there was a need. However, the distant months showed a flat trend due to foreign wheat. As a result, this month rose by 3 fen compared to the previous day, December rose by 3 fen, January fell by a small 1 fen, February rose by a large 1 fen, and March and April remained unchanged. Spot transactions were still rare, and only parcels were not opened.

Sugar Market: Coarse Sand and White Sugar Market Sentiment Improves 195

│Up 2.5 Fen│

Yesterday, the sugar market's sentiment improved as the premium (biaojin) repeatedly increased. The guild's first board price for No. 24 coarse sand white sugar was 14 taels, 8 qian, 3 fen, and 7.5 li. As outgoing stocks gradually decreased, it rose to 14 taels, 8 qian, and 5 fen, with a total increase of 2.5 fen before and after. No. 18 medium sand white sugar was 14 taels, No. 20 medium sand white sugar was 14 taels and 3 qian. New goods under the Dachang name were 14 taels, 6 qian to 6.25 fen. No. 8 Dutch red high-quality goods were 11 taels and 7 qian. No. 10 Dutch red old goods, light-colored oil-wrapped sugar, were 11 taels and 7 qian. Because they can be used to dilute foreign sugar, they were quite popular. As for Taikoo refined sugar, there were continued openings yesterday. B mark was 16 taels and 5 fen, CW mark was 15 taels and 8 qian, DY mark was 15 taels and 3 qian, HX mark was 15 taels and 1 qian, with little fluctuation.

Silk and Tea: European and American Silk Telegrams to Shanghai are Sparse 196

Yesterday, the foreign merchant silk market in this port still showed no improvement. Although there were white factory telegrams from Lyon and England to Shanghai, the number was only thirty or forty bales each, and they were spot transactions with no price increases. The attitude of various manufacturers was passive.

Needle-Shaped and Eyebrow-Shaped Green Tea Sales Are Smooth in Europe and Popular in Japan 197

Yesterday, the sales of needle-shaped and eyebrow-shaped green tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other routes continued to be smooth. British firms such as Jardine Matheson, Jinlong, Fushi, Yuansheng, and other firms had purchase interest. There were also telegrams from foreign countries requesting supply. Therefore, the market for needle-shaped eyebrows and elegant eyebrows trended firm. However, the stocks were nearly exhausted, and supply could not meet demand. As for the Zhenmei category, there were no large transactions throughout the city. The Russian Xieyi Association had little sales of Gongxi green tea.

However, firms such as Jinlong and Yongxing, seeing that tea prices were low, were eager to take the opportunity to search for goods in preparation for re-manufacturing needle-shaped eyebrows, elegant eyebrows, and other patterns to be transported to Morocco for sale.

Coal: Liu Jiang Small-Sized Coal Sales are Stagnant and Prices Fall 198

In previous years, the sales of mid-to-low-grade small-sized white coal from Liu Jiang were relatively strong in the winter because many of the water-filled coals in the major buildings in this port used it. Unexpectedly, this year, most users of water-filled coal have switched to using bituminous coal or Shanxi coal. As a result, the sales of Liu Jiang small-sized coal have become stagnant, and the market price has also fallen. Yesterday, the market price was only 5.5 taels per ton.

Hardware: No. 26 American White Iron Reaches Its Peak 199

Hardware transactions were still good yesterday. Over 600 dan of No. 16 to No. 20 new lead wires were opened for sale. However, because the market was stingy with goods, prices soared. The price per dan was 14 taels, which was 2.5 qian higher than before. No. 21 to No. 25 were still estimated at 18 taels, but there were few transactions. There were an unusual number of inquiries for American white iron, and the market was unusually strong. Among them, No. 26 was the most popular among all goods, and the market price per dan could be estimated at 18 taels and 2.5 qian, which was the highest price in more than ten years. No. 24 was 14 taels and 5 qian, No. 28 was 16 taels and 5 qian, and 48 sheets were 15 taels and 5 qian. It was found that over 270 or 280 dan were opened for sale yesterday. However, because the overseas price of this product was unusually firm, the market price in this port also showed no sign of falling. There were transactions for No. 24 to No. 28 white iron tiles, but there were no price increases or decreases. British white iron seemed to be easing yesterday, mainly because customers who had purchased goods last time had not yet sold them all. There was also a shortage of spot small-sized nails, so many merchants were interested in them. People estimated the price at 3 fen at 13 taels and 5 qian, 4 fen at 13 taels and 5 fen, 12 taels and 5 qian, and 6 fen at 12 taels. Recently, the overseas telegrams for bamboo joint steel bars have continuously raised prices, so the standard in this port has also risen rapidly. For example, 3 fen, 7 fen, and 1 inch all require 77 or 78 taels, and patterned steel can also be opened to 70 taels. The factory prices of this factory's Yuan nails have also discussed raising prices due to the high cost of raw materials. Each barrel of Beisi has risen to 6 taels and 1 qian, and exports are 6 taels and 5 qian. However, actual transactions are affected by this. Only 700 or 800 barrels have been opened for sale in recent days. There have been fewer inquiries for black iron sheets recently, and the market is also more sluggish. 3.6 feet are 8 taels and 5 qian, and 3.7 feet are 9 taels. The transactions for tinplate have been slightly less than before recently, but the market price has always been maintained and has not fallen. British goods of 90 pounds are 11 taels and 2.5 qian, 100 pounds are 12 taels, American goods are 14 taels and 5 qian, 100 pounds are 16 taels, 200 pounds of regular goods are 32 taels, secondary goods are 22 taels, 35 pounds are 39 taels and 5 qian, and 180 pounds of British iron are 22 taels and American goods are 27 taels.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Speech

Flipping Through Books 218

— Buddha

It's truly annoying to make everyday talks without a topic. Some topics are too dangerous to do, some topics are not worth doing, and some topics are unnecessary. When I woke up this morning, I flipped through the newspaper again. What was reported was the eve of the League of Nations meeting and the outbreak of the war in the Black Province. Thinking of the loyal and patriotic volunteers who were resisting the violence in the Eastern Province in this freezing weather, I wished I could fly there and help them kill the enemy. Then I saw the telegram from President Song ordering General Su Bingwen not to harm Japanese prisoners. President Song's benevolence and reputation were also rare. So I put the newspaper aside and didn't look at it.

I was very bored, so I pulled a book from the bookshelf. When I opened it, it turned out to be a copy of Zuo Zhuan. I flipped through it casually and read the passage where Duke Xiang of Song fought with the Chu people in Hong. Duke Xiang said, "In ancient times, one did not inflict a second wound, nor capture the gray-haired. The armies of ancient times did not take advantage of narrow terrain. Even though I am the remnant of a defeated country, I will not attack those who are not in formation." I laughed at Duke Xiang of Song for being so fond of practicing virtue, and for being called a hegemon for a time. Then I threw Zuo Zhuan aside and pulled a Bible from the bookshelf. Suddenly, I saw the passage, "If someone strikes my left cheek, I will offer my right cheek to him." I deeply sighed at the greatness of Jesus' teachings, but since I am not a Christian, what's the point of looking at it? So I put it aside without reading it. Still bored, I pulled out a copy of Zizhi Tongjian. Again, I saw a passage, "Lou Shide of the Tang Dynasty, whose younger brother was appointed governor of Daizhou, resigned from his post. Shide taught him to be patient. His younger brother said, 'From now on, if someone spits in my face, I will simply wipe it off.' Shide said, 'If someone spits in your face, it is because they are angry with you. Wiping it off goes against their intention. It is better to let it dry on its own.'" When I saw this, I couldn't help but admire the magnanimity of the ancients, which was the same essence as the teachings of Jesus, as if they were in complete agreement, which was quite remarkable.

I was quite pleased after reading the above two passages, so I continued to flip through it. I saw that "When Yang Zaisi was prime minister, Zhang Tongxiu, the vice minister of ceremonies, was the brother of Yi Zhizhi. Once, during a banquet, he joked to Zaisi, 'Secretary Yang, your face looks like a Korean.' Zaisi happily cut paper and put on a headscarf, reversed his purple robe, and performed a Korean dance." I secretly laughed at how there were such shameless people in ancient times, and I was greatly disappointed. I put the Tongjian back on the shelf.

I thought that I shouldn't read proper history books, and that I should look at novels instead. I casually flipped through a copy of Romance of the Western Chamber, and I was quite pleased. I thought that if I were to read Romance of the Western Chamber, I would definitely have to eat wheat porridge while reading it. I also thought that Jin Shengtan's comments on Romance of the Western Chamber were the best, so I might as well take a look at his comments. It happened to be the "torturing the beauty" section, which said, "I saw two scholars arguing about a principle in the street. They were both red-faced and furious, as if they couldn't coexist, but they still cupped their hands high and bowed low, using words like 'zhi hu zhe ye' in every sentence. Their words were thorny, and it seemed like they would never stop. Suddenly, a strong man came along, waved his arm, and shouted in the middle to resolve the situation. Isn't that satisfying!" Just as I was reading to the exciting part, I suddenly remembered that I had to make a talk today, and I didn't have a topic yet. So I wrote down the books I had just seen here in a messy manner, which can also be considered a talk.

Achievements of Lu 219

Literature

Writing Worries About My Homeland, Which is Full of Thorns 220

— Sun Choucheng

Yesterday, I was invited to a banquet by a friend, where I met an old acquaintance, Mr. So-and-so. Talking about the endless civil strife, he showed me four heptasyllabic poems he had written, titled "Writing Worries About My Homeland, Which is Full of Thorns." After reading them, I felt a tear in every word, and I couldn't help but feel sad. I asked him if he could publish them in the newspaper as a way to appeal for help. He said that he deeply wished to think about the disaster victims in his hometown, but after traveling to Shanghai, he had suffered misfortune because of his writing, so he dared not offend others with his worrying works again. I said, "Then how about not publishing your real name?" He finally agreed. Therefore, I respectfully follow his instructions and transcribe his original work as follows, hoping that the reader will understand it.

The rivers and mountains of the old country are like a game of chess,

The news that comes is extremely sad.

The shadow of a snake in the cup frightens dreams,

The rumors in the market cast the most suspicion.

When the bandits are setting fires and looting,

How many lives can we cultivate to see peace?

Crying in Changsha is of no use,

My heart is cluttered and confused.

I heard that the beacon fires are blazing in the wild pavilions,

I can't bear to watch people drunk while I alone stay awake.

The state of chaos is like the Tianbao era,

Protecting the people relies on the spirit of the land.

The murderous aura suddenly rises, whitening the suburbs,

I fear to see the burn marks on the distant green mountains.

I scratch my head in vain, seeking a safe plan,

But I'm willing to let my floating life be drunk in green.

The military letters from Yu and Shaanxi are too tense,

The Yuan Rong's small team goes out to the suburbs in a hurry.

They don't hesitate to deprive Qin of the head of the quail,

And it is difficult for me to firm my wooden intestines against the snow.

The bandits are rising in droves like thorns,

And the supply of the mighty army is exhausted.

The conscripts ask about the road ahead with hardship,

But the ever-changing situation makes them lament the unknown.

The fine guests gather at the banquet to discuss the bandit atmosphere,

And the four sides of the old mountain are filled with yellow clouds.

The villagers expect me to return in vain,

And I am ashamed to face you, for I have no way to save the disaster.

The remnant chrysanthemums are proud of the frost, their bones clear,

And the migratory geese cry at the moon, regretting leaving the flock.

I cry out in the wilderness with disheveled hair,

Why not let me be the commander?

Science

On Coal Gas Poisoning and First Aid 221

— Ren

During the cold winter months, it is a great pleasure to warm oneself around a stove or to place one in the bedroom. However, one should also be careful, otherwise one could not only burn one's clothes, but also cause death. This is not a lie. If you just take a look at the newspapers from last year or the winter before last, you can prove that what I say is true.

How exactly can coal gas cause death? This is a question worth studying. Originally, firewood or coal, under the influence of high temperature in the stove, undergoes a chemical reaction and combines with the oxygen in the air to become a colorless, odorless, and tasteless carbon dioxide gas. During the combination, it also releases a large amount of heat, so the remaining carbon also combines with oxygen due to the heat. This cycle continues until all the carbon is completely oxidized. The impurities in the fuel remain as ashes.

Carbon gasification (i.e., combustion) requires a large amount of oxygen and releases a larger amount of carbon dioxide. If the ventilation equipment is perfect, then there is no problem. Fresh air can enter from the outside as much as possible, driving out the useless dioxy-

Page 22

-de carbon. However, sometimes, in order to prevent the spread of heat, all the windows are tightly closed. In this way, all the oxygen in the room gradually decreases due to oxidation, while the useless carbon dioxide gradually increases. Everyone knows that living things cannot live without oxygen. Although carbon dioxide does not contain a trace of toxic substances, it can also make people in the room gradually feel dizzy. If you don't open the windows at this time to let fresh air in (assuming the people in the room are already fast asleep), then all the living things will suffocate and die.

But there is also one biggest reason, which is that the carbon under the stove oxidizes into carbon dioxide and rises, passing through the heated carbon at the top. Because of the lack of oxygen, it is reduced to carbon monoxide. The blue flame emitted from the stove is caused by this reaction. This carbon monoxide, although also a colorless, odorless, and tasteless gas like carbon dioxide, is not as gentle as carbon dioxide. It has strong toxicity. If the air contains one part of carbon monoxide per eight hundred parts, it can kill the people in the room within thirty minutes. This is because when it is inhaled into the lungs, it can combine with red blood cells

-to form a cherry-red substance. This substance cannot distribute nutrients to the body, so that all life is completely stopped and leads to death. Think about how scary this is. In people who die from coal poisoning, if the whole body is already purple, that is evidence that the blood has already clotted and all the blood vessels in the whole body are blocked. In this way, there is no cure. If it only appears cyan or slightly purple, you should immediately put him in a place with good air circulation, rub his whole body with a cold, damp cloth to clear the stagnant blood, and boil one tael of peach kernels, five qian of枳實, and five qian of萊服子 into a soup. Separately, use one tael of raw rhubarb to filter the juice, add it, pry open the teeth, and slowly pour it in. He will recover in about half a day. For mild poisoning, just mash a lot of radish juice, or fresh pear or lotus root juice, and pour it in a place with good air circulation. You can wake up in less than twenty minutes of poisoning. People who usually burn coal stoves often eat radishes, which can also relieve the coal toxins they are usually exposed to. Dried persimmon not only relieves coal toxins, but also prevents throat diseases next spring, so you should also eat it often.

School Photos

Room Number Thirteen 222

—Lianlian

It was the eve of a holiday, just when the cold wind was beating against the sparse curtains; In dormitory number thirteen of × School’s ×× Building, eight young men were playing poker by candlelight after the lights were turned off. In the corridor, there were also two young men silently smoking cigarettes and pacing back and forth. Sometimes they listened attentively to the sounds from downstairs, and sometimes they stared blankly out the glass window. Clearly, they seemed like guards hired to report any trouble.

× School wasn’t really that strict, and the school authorities especially neglected what went on in the dormitories. It wasn’t really a big deal that they wanted to gamble, but just to be safe, they couldn’t help but worry a little. Although in fact, the dormitory supervisor was nowhere to be found that night, it was still reassuring to gamble daringly.

Because tomorrow was a holiday, there were especially many people going home that night. Although the clinking of coins and the sounds of laughter in room number thirteen weren’t very loud, they seemed loud because it was quiet. One classmate who was loud and boisterous made it seem even louder: "Three King Ks, Ace, AQ, Two Pairs, two dollars find three dollars..." Everyone was excited and cheerful, and the smoke from the cigarettes made the room hazy, even spreading to the next room. The whole environment was one of intoxication, indulgence, corruption, and unconsciousness.

Something unexpected really did happen. At this late hour, the dormitory supervisor, Mr. ×, actually returned, reeking of alcohol. The lookouts could have seen him in theory, but because it was already past 11 o'clock, they didn't think that Mr. × would come back to school, so they joined the game and gambled intently. How would they know that Mr. × was coming upstairs? And so, a tense scene was about to begin.

Mr. × was drunk and tired, and he originally had no intention of catching anyone gambling. However, after he went to bed, the clinking of coins disturbed his sleep, so he got angry and decided to get up and catch them. However, the young students were still very alert. As soon as they heard Mr. ×'s footsteps approaching, one of them opened the door and looked outside. When he saw what was happening, he slammed the door shut tightly. The candles were blown out, and the clinking of coins and the sounds of laughter ceased. The ten of them all went to bed and pretended to be asleep silently. When Mr. × opened the door and came in to check, he couldn't see anything except for the thick, lingering smoke, which made him want to choke. He was extremely puzzled. He opened the bed curtains and checked them one by one, but they were all sleeping soundly like pigs. He knew that they were up to something, but since they weren't gambling anymore, he was happy to go back to his room and sleep peacefully. But these little guys were not to be trifled with. They thought that he had deliberately made things difficult for them, so they had to play a trick on Mr. ×, so that he wouldn't do it again in the future. Xiao Jin, nicknamed Pan Jinlian, then came up with a clever plan, which was: "The little ones use a little trick, and the teacher falls through the door."

Less than ten minutes after Mr. × returned to his room, a sudden fire alarm sounded in dormitory number thirteen, followed by two loud banging sounds on the washbasin. Mr. × was flustered and hurried out to take a look, but the outside was empty. Where was there any fire? However, since those in number thirteen were making a nuisance of things again, and they were going to make it so that he wouldn't be able to sleep all night, he had to go into number thirteen again and try to persuade them not to mess around. Unexpectedly, after entering the doorway, he wasn't careful and tripped over a bamboo pole that had been placed across the entrance, and he fell straight to the ground, knocking him senseless. However, strangely enough, the ten students in the bed mechanically got up one by one and helped him up, patted him down, and said solicitously to him: "If we had known that the teacher was coming to inspect the room, we wouldn't have gone to the trouble of setting up these petty defense measures. Mr. ×, we're really sorry!"

Mr. × shook his head, sighed, and staggered back to his room, muttering to himself, "I wonder when I'll be able to endure the hardships of this thankless job." In room number thirteen, a burst of laughter rang out, along with a sentence: "Jin's ingenious plan has brought peace to the world, allowing the teacher to fall right through the door."

Casual Talk

For the Sake of "Vases" 223

— Ren

Today, we should take off the tinted, patriarchal, and feudal glasses of tradition. We should acknowledge that men and women are absolutely equal in any position, especially in professions. If men can do something, women should also be given the opportunity and trusted to do it. In this day and age, who can deny this?

In recent years, women's professions in China have finally sprouted a little bit. In schools and hospitals, they have already given us considerable achievements. Gradually, they have also appeared in offices. Unfortunately, they quickly gained the reputation of being nothing more than decorative "vases"! ...... I am very suspicious of people in society, why are they so bored, with nothing to do after they've eaten their fill? Isn't this insulting women's personality and ruthlessly stamping out these little seedlings of women's professions?

A friend told me, "The female staff in the office simply don't know how to do things. The boss hires them just to decorate and regulate the heavy, dull, and monotonous atmosphere in the office, giving the male staff excitement and increasing work efficiency. They dress in bright colors and pose like models, aren't they just vases? Women don't live up to expectations, who can they blame for insulting them?"

Because of the two words "vases," I was really indignant for quite a while, I often cursed those boring, slanderous, and vulgar things with all my might!

Soon, Miss Xu, a young female staff member, also came to the next-door section ×× of our company's office. Her classmates all said that she was a "modern girl"... beautiful, a modern social butterfly, many young people are chasing her! As for her duties, because we are separated by a wall, I have never figured it out. Some people say that she can't even write clearly, and she is used to answer the phone, it's just a vase.

Our small editorial office, filled with a poor and sour atmosphere, has always been cold and boring. Colleagues all wear old copper-rimmed glasses and shake their heads all day long, humming and chanting non-stop. Since the modern girl came to the next door, the warm and smiling air has penetrated through the partition and invaded our editorial office. At first, I felt that it was new, fresh, and a bit inexplicably interesting; but gradually, it caused great annoyance and unease! The telephone rings madly all day long, less than a minute apart. The crisp, delicate, singing-like tone is absorbed by our hearing nerve sentence by sentence, and our thoughts are messed up. As a result, our heads are dizzy, our legs are swollen, we can't write a word, the boss has a deadline for the manuscript, and we are so anxious that we scratch our heads and ears, humming "Brain is dizzy, eyes are blurred, and mouth is difficult to speak!" So, we began to curse the vases... Vases, you are unwilling to be self-respecting, and you willingly become vulgar things!

A friend asked me: "Who is insulting women? You should recognize the 'vase', right? People don't eat their fill and specialize in boredom! You wholeheartedly speak for women, but women themselves don't live up to expectations, what else is there to say?......"

Good Business

A Thousand Percent Profit 224

— Fang Dou

Probably about a week ago. One night, Mr. Chen and I were walking idly on Jing'an Temple Road. We talked about national affairs and our respective life problems.

Suddenly, Mr. Chen abandoned me and started talking intimately with another friend. Then he beckoned me to come over and introduced me. I am not good at socializing, and I really lack the art of social etiquette. However, that friend was just the opposite of me. He asked about my name, origin, occupation, and address in great detail, as if we had known each other for a long time.

Afterwards, I almost forgot that friend's name. I only knew that that friend was from ×× County, Zhejiang Province, and is now working as a police officer in Shanghai.

The day before yesterday afternoon, I suddenly received a red invitation, which was forwarded by Mr. Chen. I thought Mr. Chen had something happy to celebrate. When I opened it, I was confused. After a long time, I remembered the police officer I met on Jing'an Temple Road. It turned out that it was his son's "soup cake celebration," inviting me to eat soup cake, which was really polite. But looking closely, there was a line of small characters at the back, which read "Banquet is held at the ancestral home in ×× County, Zhejiang Province." I thought, my luck for eating is not good. Such a long way to go, taking a boat and taking a car, just for a meal, it's not worth it.

This afternoon, Mr. Chen ran to my place and asked me if I had received a red invitation. I replied to him, "Sorry, I am a person who believes in the principle of not giving gifts in return. First, I don't have money to give gifts, and second, giving this kind of gift is meaningless. Moreover, this is obviously doing a good business with a thousand percent profit, and I don't advocate giving it even more."

Mr. Chen smiled apologetically at me and said, "Then I'm sorry to you. I already sent a four-dollar gift this morning, with the names of both of us. I'm here to inform you now, but I didn't expect you to be!!"

I had no choice but to take out two silver dollars and return them to Mr. Chen. I said with a smile: "Then, Lao Chen, he's holding the banquet at his ancestral home in ×× County, Zhejiang Province, are you going or not?"

Mr. Chen shook his head, smiled, and ran away. I thought: this good business with a thousand percent profit was finally done successfully by that friend.

Health Weekly

A Dissertation on Scarlet Fever 225

— Ji Hua

Scarlet fever is an acute infectious disease. Anyone with a little medical knowledge can understand it. However, it is really difficult to prevent the spread of scarlet fever. Because the spread of scarlet fever is unbelievably rapid. There are often cases of mutual infection along the household and in the whole area. Some even die in the evening after developing the disease in the morning, or die in the morning after developing the disease in the evening. The sudden and premature death is deeply regrettable.

The Origin of Scarlet Fever

This disease rarely occurs in autumn and summer, less often in spring, and most often in winter. The winter climate should have been cold, but it is warm instead. The Inner Canon says, "If the climate is not as it should be, it will brew evil epidemics." The throat opens into the lungs, and the pharynx opens into the stomach. The throat and pharynx are the portals of the lungs and stomach. The evil enters the lungs and stomach through the mouth and nose. Severe cold binds the exterior, and epidemic poison accumulates in the interior. It steams up in the lung and stomach meridians. The fire of the liver and gallbladder takes advantage of the situation to ascend. Thus, scarlet fever is formed.

Symptoms of Scarlet Fever

The symptoms of scarlet fever are high fever, red face, soreness throughout the body, and rotten throat, making swallowing difficult. The rash first appears on the head and face, and then on the chest and ribs. This is the correct symptom of scarlet fever. If there is no sweat after treatment, and the rash cannot penetrate and present a depressed appearance, with a foul voice and rapid breathing, it is difficult to treat.

Differential Diagnosis of Scarlet Fever

There are differences between epidemic throat, diphtheria, throat wind, and throat blockage. There are differences between true rash, wind rash, red rash, and measles rash. Single throat symptoms without rash, or single rash without throat symptoms, cannot be called scarlet fever. Scarlet fever is a kind of epidemic evil, which cannot be compared with ordinary throat and rash symptoms. Only when rash and throat symptoms appear at the same time can it be called scarlet fever.

Children and Scarlet Fever

Children's bodies are not fully developed, and their internal organs are delicate and weak, making them susceptible to seasonal evils. However, there are also cases of single rash, with slight sore throat, but no rot. This is due to latent heat in the womb, which is triggered by seasonal evils, and is not contagious scarlet fever. The symptoms are generally fever, cough, irritability, and nausea. If throat rot is seen, and the rash is faintly visible, it is scarlet fever. It is urgent to seek medical treatment.

Prevention of Scarlet Fever

Scarlet fever is a very dangerous disease, as detailed above. Now, I will briefly write down the prevention methods below. I think readers will also be happy to hear them. If neighbors or relatives have scarlet fever, do not enthusiastically visit them. If family members have scarlet fever, they must also be isolated in separate rooms. All the patient's food utensils, clothing, and other items must not be mixed together. Often decoct radish in water as a substitute for tea. Olives are also acceptable. The indoor air must always be circulating. The stool must always be kept smooth.

Treatment of Scarlet Fever

At the beginning of scarlet fever, it is necessary to quickly induce sweating. Therefore, first use the sweating method, then use the clearing method, or use the purging method. It must be divided into three stages: initial, middle, and late. In qi, in ying, or more in qi, or more in ying. The pulse is uncertain. The diagnosis should be accurate. If there is any inappropriateness, it is often a fact. My ancestor, Gong, had 20 years of experience in scarlet fever. The scarlet fever he treated was all effective. Now, I record the various prescriptions prescribed by my ancestor below, so that readers can follow the map and find something to refer to.

(1) Antitoxin and Rash-Transmitting Decoction

Specially treats measles rash at the beginning, aversion to cold and fever, swollen and painful throat, hindering swallowing, soreness throughout the body, chest pain, and nausea.

Spike of Schizonepeta tenuifolia, half a mace of dried root cast-off shells of cicada, eight fen of tender Belamcanda chinensis, one mace of licorice, five fen of Pueraria lobata, two mace of Arctium lappa, two mace of light Sclerotium Poriae Cocos, eight fen of Platycodon grandiflorus, one mace of Mentha haplocalyx, one and a half mace of Forsythia suspensa, two mace of Bombyx batryticatus, three mace of Glycine max (black), three mace of fresh bamboo shavings, two mace of Lemna minor, three mace. If nausea is severe and the tongue coating is white and greasy, add four fen of Yushu Dan to be taken with boiled water.

(2) Modified Mahuang Xingren Shigao Decoction

Specially treats measles rash that cannot be transmitted, aversion to cold and fever, swollen and painful throat, or white rotten inner gate, or severe symptoms of cough and Qi ascending.

Ephedra sinica, four fen of Gypsum fibrosum, four mace of Fritillaria thunbergii, three mace of fresh bamboo leaves, thirty sheets of Semen Armeniacae Amarum, three mace of Belamcanda chinensis, eight fen of Bombyx batryticatus, three mace of white Raphanus sativus juice, one tael of licorice, six fen of Forsythia suspensa, two mace of Mentha haplocalyx, one mace of Radix Scrophulariae ningpoensis, one and a half mace.

(3) Modified Shengma Gegen Decoction

Specially treats measles rash that is distributed, but the head and face are unique, and there is no rash on the nose. There is fever and diarrhea, and the throat is painful but not rotten.

Rhizoma Cimicifugae, five fen of licorice, five fen of Forsythia suspensa, two mace of Bombyx batryticatus, three mace of Pueraria lobata, one and a half mace of Platycodon grandiflorus, one mace of Flos Lonicerae Japonicae, three mace of Dried Lotus Leaf, one angle of Mentha haplocalyx, eight fen of Radix Paeoniae Rubra, two mace of dried root cast-off shells of cicada, eight fen of Citrus aurantium, three mace.

(4) Modified Black Ointment Decoction

Specially treats the evil of the epidemic that cannot be reached, destroys yin fluid, measles rash is distributed but not transmitted, fever without sweat, swollen and red throat, dry pain and white rot, dry mouth and irritability, red tongue with thorns, or severe symptoms of black tongue without saliva.

Glycine max (black), three mace of Mentha haplocalyx, eight fen of Forsythia suspensa, three mace of Bombyx batryticatus, three mace of fresh Radix Rehmanniae glutinosae, four mace of Gypsum fibrosum, four mace of Radix Paeoniae Rubra, two mace of dried root cast-off shells of cicada, eight fen of fresh Herba Dendrobii, four mace of licorice, six fen of Fritillaria thunbergii, three mace of Lemna minor, three mace of fresh bamboo leaves, thirty sheets of Rhizoma Imperatae cylindricae, one tael each.

A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis 226

— Xi Yi

Definition

A persistent cough that does not heal and exhibits symptoms of fatigue is called pulmonary tuberculosis.

Causes

There are three causes of pulmonary tuberculosis: one is due to external influences, one is due to internal injuries, and one is due to heredity. Those due to external influences are caused by catching a cold or being forced by cold weather, and the lung qi is threatened. If it does not heal for a long time, it will turn into pulmonary tuberculosis. Those due to internal injuries are caused by working all day long, not being able to enjoy sunlight and fresh air sufficiently, and the food is lacking in nourishment, so the lungs are gradually damaged and lose their resistance, and it turns into pulmonary tuberculosis. Those due to heredity are caused by the lung tuberculosis virus of the parents being transmitted to the child's body. As the child's body grows, the virus also deepens. Often, they die at the age of eighteen or nineteen.

Symptoms

The symptoms of pulmonary tuberculosis are divided into three stages. The first stage: cough and chest pain. The second stage: cough and chest pain with shortness of breath and hemoptysis. The third stage: cough and chest pain, shortness of breath, hemoptysis, flushed cheeks, and foul voice, all symptoms are present.

Pathology

Western medicine discusses pulmonary tuberculosis, focusing on Mycobacterium tuberculosis. Mycobacterium tuberculosis is shaped like a thin rod, about one-third the length of a red blood cell. It has a fatty or waxy substance on the outside. When I read Chao Yuanfang's "Origins of Diseases," it also says that lung worms are like silkworms. It can be seen that there is no doubt that lung tuberculosis has worms. However, since lung tuberculosis is a kind of bacteria, the bacteria in the patient's sputum are left in the dust and spread with the wind. Everyone has the opportunity to be infected with pulmonary tuberculosis. Why do those who are sick get sick, and those who are not sick never get sick? This is because the human body's resistance is strong, and the virus is not easy to sneak in. Try to see the symptoms of those who died of lung disease. It must be from shallow to deep, from gradual to severe. It will never be the case that once you have lung tuberculosis, the symptoms of the third stage will appear immediately.

Treatment

The most important treatment for pulmonary tuberculosis is cough, because the lungs' inhalation and exhalation have a certain normal state. If there is an obstacle in the lungs, the lung qi cannot follow the normal breathing, so it starts a counter-reaction and coughs frequently. However, the cough should also be observed for fierceness and gentleness. A fierce cough indicates a mild illness and can be treated with drugs that promote lung function. A gentle cough indicates a more serious illness and can be treated with products that clear the lungs and resolve phlegm, making it easier to expectorate the phlegm. If the cough shows symptoms such as hemoptysis, shortness of breath, foul voice, and bone steaming, it indicates that the deficiency has appeared. It is necessary to use large doses of products that tonify and purify the lungs to protect the vital energy. When the vital energy is restored, then circulate and regulate with products that clear, purify, and nourish the lungs, so that the virus is completely eliminated and it will heal on its own. If the vital energy has been lost in the third stage of lung disease and the spleen and stomach are also unable to digest, no matter how many wonderful methods there are, it will be difficult to hope for recovery.

Health Consultant Regulations 227

(1) The purpose of this publication is to serve social health and popularize medical knowledge to the public.

(2) All difficult medical questions, such as the principles of diseases, patient care, disease prevention, medical treatment policies, and distinctions of medicinal properties, will be answered in detail when inquiries are sent by letter.

(3) Letters answered by this publication will be disclosed in this publication or directly answered by letter from this office.

(4) For extremely complex and difficult questions in the letters, it is necessary to search medical books extensively, consult widely, or slightly delay the reply.

(5) Letters with unclear descriptions and ambiguous meanings will not be answered. Cases of critical illness requiring prescriptions will not be answered. Requests to review and determine the right and wrong of prescriptions will not be answered.

(6) All letters requesting a reply must clearly state the address in detail. Those without details will not be answered.

(7) All letters must be written on Chinese-style envelopes and the font must be neat. A return postage stamp of one dime and two cents must be attached.

Common Knowledge of Blood Diseases: A Series of Talks on Blood Diseases (1) 228

— Ding Ji Hua

The human body's organization, from the outer skin and muscles to the inner bones and internal organs, all rely on blood for nourishment. If the blood is weak, the skin and muscles will be dry and rough, and the bones and internal organs will be cramped and hard. If we want a healthy body, how can it be like a tree without roots, and expect it to be lush and verdant? The ancient sages said that food enters the stomach, is steamed and transformed into liquid, which is transported upward by the lungs and distributed to the lungs. The lungs are in charge of distribution, sprinkling on the internal organs and moistening the skin and hair. When the liquid is full, it becomes blood. When the blood is full, it becomes flesh. It can be seen that liquid is the essence of food, and blood is brewed from the body fluids. But if there is no qi to supply its operation, then the circulation up and down, how can it be smooth? Therefore, in Chinese medical knowledge, there is a clear statement that qi is the commander of blood, and treating blood first treats qi. It is true that blood cannot flow by itself and must rely on qi to move it. Qi weakness causes blood stagnation. Qi deficiency causes blood loss. Qi reversal causes blood disorder. Qi forcing causes blood to run wild. Qi knotting causes blood coagulation. Qi rush causes blood to burst out. Therefore, qi is to blood as shrimp is to jellyfish. People with abundant qi and full blood have plump muscles and shiny faces. It is said that they are energetic and radiant. Using qi to make blood move, and blood to guard qi, using each other for each other, no disease can invade and no external feeling can Gong. The camp guard is peaceful, and the Yin and Yang are harmonious. It is a healthy body. If qi is exhausted and blood is weak, the dryness of hair and skin and the darkness of appearance are self-evident. Moreover, the face may be yellow and puffy, the muscles may be reduced, the actions may be panting, and the weakness may be powerless. There is little diet, and digestion is poor. Both stools are difficult, and dragons and thunder are easy to rebel. It is said that the internal organs are truly deficient and the resistance is weak. Even if there is no external trouble, there is also concern that changes will occur suddenly between the elbows and armpits.

Therefore, those who are good at nourishing life must be good at nourishing their blood in order to maintain their health. If you want to nourish your blood, you must be good at regulating your qi. Clear qi, clear blood. Turbid qi, turbid blood. Decayed food, foul air, and those who mix into the qi will also escape into the blood. If the blood is not clear, all kinds of diseases will gather together. This is because there is less nourishing qi and more carbon gas. The Western theory says that venous blood cells are mostly purple and dark, and arterial blood cells are mostly bright red. Venous blood contains more carbon gas, and arterial blood contains more nourishing qi. There are also white blood cells that can eat the micro-bacteria that invade blood vessels, also known as phagocytes, which are extremely viscous in nature. I will not discuss them in detail here.

Generally speaking, the blood in the human body absorbs nourishing qi and returns to the arteries. If there is more nourishing qi and less carbon gas, the blood will be pure and clean, and the body will be light and healthy. There is a possibility of avoiding disease. On the contrary, hoping for health and freedom from disease is impossible. However, the arrival of the disease is not an end. Confused talk of blood loss, anemia, and women's metrorrhagia, etc. Analyzed talk of many signs. But the outline of the discussion is no more than three causes. One day is external cause. External blood diseases mostly belong to Yang evil. The Yin is deficient first, and the wind, heat, dryness, and fire of the weather take advantage of the deficiency to invade. If it is forced to the lungs and stomach, and it goes to the clear path, it is nosebleed. If it goes to the turbid path, it is hematemesis, vomiting blood, etc. If it is forced to the intestines, the network qi is not stable, it is bloody dysentery, intestinal deviation, etc. The second day is internal cause. Internal blood diseases are nothing more than anger, depression, stimulating the liver, laboring the body and thinking bitterly, consuming the heart and spleen, indulging in desires to kill kidney Yin, and indulging in emotions to raise true fire. If the fire is inflamed above, the blood goes upward. If the fire is corrected below, the blood flows downward. The third day is neither internal nor external cause. Blood that is neither internal nor external cause is all due to improper diet and excessive labor. Mr. Ye Xiangyan said that smoking and spicy food release the lungs, and alcohol and food harm the stomach. The sun finally spins, and the evil fire is strong inside, as well as falling, beating, and working too hard, causing the blood vessels to rupture and the circulation to be off track. If it bursts upward, it is vomiting. If it flows downward, it is diarrhea. For women, it is collapse. The above are the outlines of the main points of argument. Enumerated separately. There are many items of symptoms. Listed at the bottom. In order to become the present. Fortunately, give me your teachings.
